### [81] [ClaimDiff-RL: Fine-Grained Caption Reinforcement Learning through Visual Claim Comparison](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20278)
*Tianle Li,Xuyang Shen,Yan Ma,Rongxin Guo,Shaoxiang Chen,Jiacheng Chen,Haochen Wang,Hongyang Tang,Yucong Zhou,Yu Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了ClaimDiff-RL，通过将图像描述分解为可验证的原子声明差异，解决了长文本描述中奖励粒度过粗导致幻觉与遗漏无法权衡的问题，实现了更细粒度且可诊断的强化学习训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的强化学习（RL）方法通常将长文本描述视为单一序列进行打分，导致幻觉（hallucination）错误和重要信息遗漏（omission）被混合，难以平衡描述的“忠实度”与“信息完整度”。传统的整体标量奖励掩盖了局部错误，限制了模型在复杂场景描述中的表现。

Method: 提出了ClaimDiff-RL框架。该框架引入多模态裁判（multimodal judge），对模型生成的描述与参考描述进行对比，分解为基于视觉证据的原子声明差异。通过验证这些差异，并赋予不同错误类型（如幻觉、遗漏）及严重程度，将其转化为细粒度的奖励信号，从而实现对模型训练的精确指导。

Result: 实验证明，ClaimDiff-RL显著改善了幻觉与遗漏之间的平衡。在多项基准测试及人工评测中，该方法不仅提升了模型处理细节的能力，在物体计数、空间关系和场景识别等细粒度能力维度上，甚至超越了Gemini-3-Pro-Preview模型。

Conclusion: 研究表明，使用基于原子声明差异（atomic claim differences）的细粒度奖励机制，能够有效解决长文本图像描述中的“忠实度”与“信息完整度”之间的权衡难题。这种可诊断、可验证的奖励建模方法是提升大规模视觉语言模型生成质量的关键，优于传统的整体式标量奖励方法。

Abstract: Long-form image captioning exposes a reward granularity problem in RL: captions are judged as whole sequences, while the important errors occur at the level of individual visual claims. A good dense caption should be both faithful and informative, avoiding hallucination without omitting salient details. Yet pairwise preferences, reference-based metrics, and holistic scalar rewards compress these local errors into a single sequence-level signal, obscuring the tradeoff between factuality and coverage. We introduce ClaimDiff-RL, a framework that uses reference-conditioned atomic claim differences as the reward unit for caption RL. Given an image, an actor caption, and a reference caption, a multimodal judge enumerates visually grounded differences, verifies each difference against the image, assigns open-vocabulary error types and severity levels, and produces per-difference statistics for reward composition. This makes hallucinated claims and omitted salient facts separately measurable and tunable. Experiments show that holistic scalar rewards can reduce hallucination by increasing missing facts, while ClaimDiff-RL exposes this faithfulness and coverage tradeoff and enables more balanced operating points. On a 160-image human-labeled diagnostic benchmark, public captioning benchmarks, and VQA benchmarks, ClaimDiff-RL improves the hallucination--missing-fact balance, preserves general capability, and even surpasses Gemini-3-Pro-Preview on several fine-grained Capability dimensions such as object counting, spatial relations, and scene recognition. These results suggest that typed, verifiable claim differences are an effective reward unit for fine-grained and diagnosable caption RL.

### [82] [Introspective X Training: Feedback Conditioning Improves Scaling Across all LLM Training Stages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20285)
*Brandon Cui,Ximing Lu,Jaehun Jung,Syeda Nahida Akter,Hyunwoo Kim,Yuxiao Qu,David Acuna,Shrimai Prabhumoye,Yejin Choi,Prithviraj Ammanabrolu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种“内省训练”（IXT）技术，通过引入奖励模型对数据进行质量标注，并让预训练模型根据反馈进行差异化学习，成功将训练效率提升了 2.8 倍，并显著增强了模型在数学和编程任务中的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型（LLM）的训练管线冗长且计算成本高昂，旨在解决如何通过跨阶段的反馈机制提升整体训练效率，即利用模型后期的训练动态信息来优化早期的预训练过程。

Method: 提出了一种名为“内省训练”（Introspective Training, IXT）的新方法。该方法借鉴了离线奖励条件强化学习的思路，利用一个“思维奖励模型”对数据进行自然语言评论标注。在后续训练中，模型通过读取这些前缀条件反馈来区分数据质量，从而在预训练阶段就开始进行质量感知的差异化学习。

Result: 在从头训练 7.5B 到 12B 参数量、处理 18 万亿 token 的实验中，IXT 方法展现了显著优势：模型在通用计算效率上提升了高达 2.8 倍，并在数学和代码等复杂领域达到了常规训练方法无法企及的性能水平。

Conclusion: Introspective Training (IXT) 证明了利用训练后期阶段的反馈机制指导早期预训练的可行性。通过在预训练阶段引入基于质量的标注和前缀条件控制，可以显著提升大模型的训练效率和最终性能，为打破计算资源瓶颈提供了新的研究范式。

Abstract: We tackle the question of how to scale more efficiently across the many, ever-growing stages of current LLM training pipelines. Our guiding intuition stems from the fact that the dynamics of later stages of the pipeline, e.g. post-training, can be used to inform earlier stages such as pre-training. To this end, we propose Introspective Training (or IXT), inspired by offline reward-conditioned reinforcement learning and applicable to any stage of training. IXT uses a thinking reward model to annotate data with natural language critique based feedback, enabling quality aware training from the earliest stages of the pipeline. Models are then trained by prefix-conditioning the data with the generated feedback -- ensuring that not all tokens are treated equally starting much earlier in training than usual. Comprehensive experiments on 7.5-12B transformer-based dense LLMs trained from scratch all the way up to 18 Trillion tokens seen show that our method: bends scaling curves resulting in up to 2.8x more compute efficiency generally; and reaches performance levels unachievable for models trained otherwise in domains such as math and code.

### [83] [Weasel: Out-of-Domain Generalization for Web Agents via Importance-Diversity Data Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20291)
*Fatemeh Pesaran zadeh,Seyeon Choi,Xing Han Lù,Siva Reddy,Gunhee Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 Weasel，一种网页智能体的高效离线训练框架。通过轨迹选择算法、AXTree 剪枝和风格对齐推理，在大幅降低训练成本的同时提升了模型的跨域泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有网页智能体在特定任务和领域上微调后，缺乏跨域泛化能力；且离线训练时存在大量冗余轨迹和过长的辅助可访问树（AXTree）状态，导致计算资源消耗巨大，效率低下。

Method: 1. 轨迹选择：使用贪婪算法平衡步长的重要性与多样性，在有限的预算内选择最优轨迹；2. AXTree 剪枝：基于目标中心策略，仅保留 ground-truth 动作相关的上下文，减少输入冗余；3. 风格对齐：将专家轨迹中的指令替换为模型生成的、与其推理风格一致的理性分析（rationales）。

Result: 在 WebArena、WorkArena 和 MiniWob 等评测基准上，Weasel 在使用 Qwen2.5-7B、Gemma3-4B 和 Qwen3-8B 等模型时，显著提升了跨域性能，并将离线训练速度提升了约 9.7 至 12.5 倍。

Conclusion: Weasel 提供了一种高效且具有泛化能力的网页智能体训练方案。通过轨迹选择、AXTree 剪枝和风格一致性推理，不仅显著降低了离线训练的计算成本，还增强了模型在未见域的性能，为大规模网页智能体开发提供了实用工具。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have enabled web agents that follow natural language goals through multi-step browser interactions. However, agents fine-tuned on specific trajectories and domain often struggle to generalize out of domain, and offline training can be compute-inefficient due to noisy, redundant trajectories and long accessibility-tree (AXTree) states. To address both issues, we propose Weasel, a trajectory selection method for offline training of web agents. Weasel selects a fixed-budget subset of trajectory steps by optimizing an objective that balances unary importance with pairwise diversity over states, websites, and interaction patterns, solving efficiently with a greedy algorithm. We further improve efficiency with target-centered AXTree pruning that keeps only content around the ground-truth action target, and we mitigate style mismatch for reasoning-native models by replacing expert traces with model-generated, style-consistent rationales. Across AgentTrek and NNetNav training datasets, evaluations in WebArena, WorkArena, and MiniWob, and experiments with Qwen2.5-7B, Gemma3-4B, and Qwen3-8B, Weasel improves out-of-domain performance while reducing training cost, producing roughly 9.7-12.5$\times$ training speedups over standard fine-tuning. We make the code available at https://github.com/fatemehpesaran310/weasel.

</details>


### [84] [TreeText-CTS: Compact, Source-Traceable Tree-Path Evidence for Irregular Clinical Time-Series Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20292)
*Kwanhyung Lee,Juhwan Choi,Jongheon Kim,Joohyung Lee,Hyeongwon Jang,Eunho Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TreeText-CTS是一种将临床时间序列转化为人类可读且可追溯的决策树路径证据的新方法，在显著提升EHR模型可解释性的同时，实现了超越现有文本接口的预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的数值时间序列模型虽性能优异但缺乏可解释性，而现有的文本化接口要么因冗余导致信息过载，要么因自由文本摘要而难以追溯至原始临床测量数据。本文旨在桥接临床时间序列数据的可解释性与高预测性能之间的差距。

Method: 1. 将不规则EHR轨迹转化为紧凑的、源可追溯的树路径证据单位。
2. 利用冻结的XGBoost模型处理多尺度窗口摘要。
3. 将激活的决策树路径转化为确定性的阈值条件文本。
4. 使用证据选择器筛选关键信息，并通过语言模型编码器整合进行最终预测，无需自回归解码。

Abstract: Numerical time-series models can effectively process irregular electronic health record (EHR) trajectories, but they do not naturally expose the measurements and temporal patterns supporting each risk estimate as readable evidence. Existing text-based interfaces improve readability, but typically rely on either raw serialization, which is lengthy and redundant, or patient-level free-form summaries, which are difficult to trace to source measurements and time windows. To bridge this gap, we introduce TreeText-CTS (Clinical Time-Series), which converts irregular EHR trajectories into human-readable, compact, source-traceable tree-path evidence units without patient-level summarization or inference-time autoregressive decoding. TreeText-CTS routes multi-scale window summaries through frozen XGBoost models and verbalizes activated tree paths as deterministic, source-traceable evidence units composed of threshold conditions. An evidence selector assembles an informative subset of these units, which a language-model encoder then integrates for prediction. Across PhysioNet 2012 mortality, MIMIC-III mortality, and PhysioNet 2019 sepsis-onset forecasting, TreeText-CTS achieves the best AUROC and AUPRC among evaluated text-based EHR time-series interfaces, improving AUPRC by 6.0 to 9.7 absolute percentage points over the strongest prior text-based interface while remaining competitive with numerical time-series models. Ablations show that tree-path evidence construction, evidence selection, and language-model composition each contribute to performance. Because every span passed to the language-model encoder is constructed from activated tree-path threshold conditions, TreeText-CTS makes the evidence supplied to the final predictor inspectable and source-traceable.

### [85] [Spectral Unforgetting: Post-Hoc Recovery of Damaged Capabilities Without Retraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20296)
*Aarash Abro,Muhammad Tahir*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对语言模型微调带来的灾难性遗忘问题，本文提出了 DG-Hard 算法，通过对权重更新矩阵进行 SVD 谱滤波处理，无需额外数据即可有效修复模型在微调中意外损失的通用能力与安全对齐性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在对语言模型进行微调时，模型往往会遭遇“灾难性遗忘”，即在微调任务性能提升的同时，其他未在微调数据中显式涉及的通用能力遭受不必要的降级。作者旨在开发一种无需原始数据、仅依赖模型权重检查点的后验修复方案，以在保留微调任务增益的同时，恢复被损害的模型能力。

Method: 本文提出了 DG-Hard 方法。该方法仅需预训练模型 $W_{\mathrm{base}}$ 和微调后模型 $W_{\mathrm{ft}}$，将微调产生的权重更新量 $\Delta = W_{\mathrm{ft}} - W_{\mathrm{base}}$ 视为低秩任务信号与 IID 噪声的叠加。通过对权重增量矩阵的奇异值分解（SVD），应用 Donoho-Gavish 硬阈值策略，滤除噪声谱分量，保留关键的结构化高能量更新。此外，作者还引入了一种基于分区的条件评估指标，以精确衡量模型的修复、保持和留存效果。

Result: 在 14 种模型与任务设置及 9 项跨领域基准测试中，DG-Hard 表现出最强的综合修复能力。实验证明，该方法不仅能有效恢复因微调而退化的通用能力，且在无需额外对齐数据的情况下，成功修复了被微调损害的安全对齐水平。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种无需原始数据即可修复语言模型灾难性遗忘的方法。研究表明，微调过程中产生的性能损失并非总是不可避免的专业化代价，而是可以通过对权重更新矩阵进行谱滤波来修复的“谱残留”。DG-Hard 方法在保持目标任务性能的同时，能有效恢复被破坏的通用能力和安全对齐。

Abstract: Fine-tuning a language model for a target task routinely degrades capabilities the training data never explicitly threatened. We study this phenomenon, known as catastrophic forgetting, and propose a post-hoc repair solution that uses only the pretrained checkpoint $W_{\mathrm{base}}$ and its fine-tuned descendant $W_{\mathrm{ft}}$. The goal is not merely to revert the model toward the base checkpoint, but to recover capabilities damaged by fine-tuning while preserving both the target-task gains and any beneficial held-out improvements. We introduce DG-Hard, a checkpoint-only spectral repair method for the fine-tuning update $Δ= W_{\mathrm{ft}} - W_{\mathrm{base}}$. DG-Hard treats $Δ$ as a low-rank task-aligned signal embedded in an IID-like noise residual that gradient descent has no incentive to remove, and applies the Donoho-Gavish hard singular-value threshold to each weight-delta matrix, keeping the structured high-energy part of the update and removing the spectral bulk. This reduces repair to a closed-form SVD filtering step requiring no data-dependent tuning. A central difficulty is evaluation: average accuracy hides per-benchmark failures, while naive recovery scores reward models that simply revert toward the base. We therefore introduce a partition-conditional metric that separately tracks healing, preservation, non-damage, and target-task retention. Across $14$ (model, task) settings and nine cross-domain held-out benchmarks, DG-Hard achieves the strongest balanced repair among post-hoc baselines. DG-Hard also restores safety alignment degraded by benign fine-tuning on three independent safety axes, despite using no alignment data. These results suggest that part of fine-tuning-induced capability loss is not an unavoidable consequence of specialization, but a removable spectral residue in the weight update itself.

</details>


### [86] [Mechanisms of Misgeneralization in Physical Sequence Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20299)
*Kento Nishi,Raphael Tang,Karun Kumar,Core Francisco Park,Hidenori Tanaka*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了生成式模型在物理规划任务中分布不匹配的问题（物理泛化失效），证明了这是由局部模型误差累积导致的，并提出了一种基于数据偏差核的校准方法来修正生成分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在机器人技术和物理模拟中，生成式模型常用于路径规划，但研究人员发现，模型在训练时虽设定了特定的物理量分布（如行程距离或能量分布），但在实际生成过程中，这些物理量的 aggregate 分布往往会发生偏差，即出现“物理泛化失效（physical misgeneralization）”。本文旨在探讨这一现象的深层机制并提出缓解方案。

Method: 本文首先通过受控合成任务分析了模型误差随轨迹生成过程的累积效应，提出了“数据偏差核（data deviation kernel）”来量化预测误差对物理量分布的影响；最后基于该机制提出了一种核信息辅助的干预方法，用于校准生成模型的输出分布。

Result: 实验结果表明，物理泛化失效源于模型内部的局部预测误差在物理测量过程中的累积与传播。研究验证了数据偏差核能够准确预测哪些物理量在生成过程中会出现分布坍塌或溢出，且基于此核的干预方法能有效修复模型在迷宫导航和双摆运动任务中的分布偏差。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了生成式序列模型在物理任务中存在“物理泛化失效”现象，即虽然模型生成的个体轨迹看似合理，但其整体分布未能准确反映物理量的统计特征。通过分析模型误差传播机制，作者提出了有效的校准干预策略，为构建更符合物理规律的生成模型提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Generative sequence models are often trained to plan motion in physical domains, from robotics to mechanical simulations. When constructing a dataset to train such a model, engineers may curate demonstrations to specify how trajectories should be distributed over a physical quantity like travel distance or mechanical energy. For example, a roboticist building a maze navigation agent might choose demonstrations whose travel distances cover a fixed range uniformly, hoping to constrain the agent's expected power usage. We find that standard deep learning can violate this intent: each generated trajectory can seem plausible on its own, but the aggregate distribution over the physical quantity is wrong. We call this failure physical misgeneralization, and develop an account of its mechanism. Using controlled synthetic tasks, we show that physical misgeneralization arises when local errors typical of the model class propagate through the physical measurement to shift the recovered distribution. We estimate these errors with a data deviation kernel, and we use it to predict which physical quantities gain or lose mass in both our synthetic and more applied maze navigation and double-pendulum motion tasks. Finally, our mechanistic interpretation helps identify which mitigation strategies are structurally promising, and we use it to propose a kernel-informed intervention.

To efficiently address the resulting nonconvex optimization problem, we develop a gradient-based algorithm equipped with a backtracking line-search strategy that ensures stable and efficient convergence. In addition, we present a sensitivity analysis of the $\ell_p^p$ and $\ell_2$ loss functions, elucidating their distinct behaviors under varying noise characteristics. Extensive numerical experiments corroborate the theoretical analysis and demonstrate that the proposed approach consistently outperforms existing methods in terms of robustness and reconstruction accuracy.

Abstract: Airfoil shape design is a fundamental task in aerospace engineering, with a direct impact on flight stability and fuel consumption. They offer little control over the generated shapes, yielding invalid geometries, and they typically do not condition effectively on aerodynamic performance. To address these issues, this paper proposes AirfoilGen, a valid-by-construction and performance-aware latent diffusion model for airfoil. It first introduces a novel airfoil representation scheme, the circle sweeping representation, to constrain the generative process so that output shapes respect essential airfoil characteristics. It then enables explicit control over aerodynamic performance (e.g., lift and drag coefficients) by operating in a learned latent space: a transformer model encodes airfoil shapes into vector embeddings, and a conditional diffusion model denoises Gaussian noise into these latent embeddings while incorporating target aerodynamic performance. In addition, this paper presents a new dataset of over 200,000 airfoils, which is substantially larger than the widely used UIUC airfoil dataset (1,650 airfoils) and more suitable for training modern deep generative models. Experiments demonstrate that AirfoilGen enables airfoil generation with far greater geometric validity and aerodynamic performance controllability than previously achievable, with an average performance-conditioning accuracy of 98.41%.

### [89] [Less Data, Faster Training: repeating smaller datasets speeds up learning via sampling biases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20314)
*Jingwen Liu,Ezra Edelman,Surbhi Goel,Bingbin Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了“小样本重复训练优于大数据集训练”的计算效率之谜，发现通过小数据集引入的采样偏差能促进模型层级生长，从而为推理任务提供更有利的优化诱导偏置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在揭示为何在许多算法任务、架构和优化器中，使用较小数据集进行多次重复训练，往往比使用大数据集训练能以更少的计算量获得更好的效果。这一现象在现有理论中无法得到合理解释，因此作者希望通过探索“小数据集与大数据集差距”背后的机制来填补这一空白。

Method: 研究者通过理论分析和多项实证干预实验，探讨了“小数据集重复训练”与“大数据集训练”之间的计算效率差异。核心机制在于分析采样偏差如何促进模型在训练过程中实现更有效的层级生长（layer-wise growth）。

Result: 实验表明，较小数据集上的重复训练确实能够通过特定的采样偏差加速模型优化过程。这种速度提升在推理任务中尤为显著，证明了在特定条件下，利用小数据集进行多次重复不仅能节省计算资源，还能提升模型的学习效果。

Conclusion: 本研究提出，在数据有限的情况下，通过在较小数据集上进行多次重复训练，不仅是一种权宜之计，更可以作为一种主动的优化策略。这种策略能通过采样偏差促成更有利的层级生长，从而在推理任务中表现出更好的优化诱导偏置。

Abstract: This work investigates the ``small-vs-large gap'', where repeating on fewer samples can lead to compute saving during training compared to using a larger dataset. This is observed across algorithmic tasks, architectures and optimizers and cannot be explained using prior theory. We argue that the speedup comes from appropriate layer-wise growth enabled by sampling biases, which is more pronounced when the dataset size is smaller. We provide both theoretical analysis and empirical evidence from various interventions. Our results suggest that using a smaller dataset with more repetitions is not just a fallback strategy under data scarcity, but can be proactively leveraged as a favorable inductive biases for optimization, particularly in reasoning tasks.

### [90] [Causal Unlearning in Collaborative Optimization: Exact and Approximate Influence Reversal under Adversarial Contributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20341)
*Ali Mahdavi,Azadeh Zamanifar,Amirfarhad Farhadi,Omid Kashefi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决联邦学习中数据删除的高昂计算成本问题，本文提出了 HF-KCU 方法，通过克雷洛夫子空间近似和因果加权技术，实现了高效且精确的机器学习遗忘，在大幅提升速度的同时保持了模型精度与隐私安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着隐私法规（如 GDPR）的实施，联邦学习系统必须支持数据删除（Machine Unlearning）请求。然而，传统的重新训练方法计算成本极其高昂，难以满足生产环境的需求。

Method: 提出了 HF-KCU 方法，利用共轭梯度法在克雷洛夫子空间中近似影响函数（Influence Function），将计算复杂度从 O(d^3) 降低至 O(kd)；引入因果加权机制（Causal Weighting Mechanism）确保仅对持有被删除数据的客户端进行参数更新，并设计了针对对抗性扰动的稳健性策略。

Result: 在多个数据集和模型架构（如 ResNet-18、ViT-Lite）上验证，HF-KCU 在 CIFAR-10 上实现了 47.75 倍的加速，且测试精度仅下降 0.60%；成员推理攻击成功率降至 0.499，证明了其有效的隐私保护能力。

Conclusion: HF-KCU 是一种高效且隐私安全的联邦学习遗忘方法，通过克雷洛夫子空间近似和因果加权机制，实现了在不重新训练的情况下精确移除特定客户端数据，满足了隐私合规性要求并保证了模型性能。

Abstract: Federated learning systems must support data deletion requests to comply with privacy regulations, yet retraining from scratch after each deletion is computationally prohibitive. We present HF-KCU, a method that removes a client's contribution by approximating the influence function through conjugate gradient iterations in Krylov subspaces, reducing complexity from O(d^3) to O(kd) where k<<d.A causal weighting mechanism ensures that only clients holding the deleted data receive parameter updates, preventing spurious changes to unaffected clients. Our method is designed to handle bounded adversarial perturbations to the Hessian and gradient, providing graceful degradation under realistic threat models. We validate HF-KCU across convolutional (ResNet-18, SimpleCNN) and transformer (ViT-Lite) architectures on CIFAR-10, MNIST, and Fashion-MNIST. On CIFAR-10 under Dirichlet (alpha=0.5) partitioning, HF-KCU achieves 47.75 times speedup over retraining while maintaining test accuracy within 0.60% of the rational baseline(71.16 vs 71.76 %). Membership inference attacks on the forget set yield success rates of 0.499 matching the retrained model and confirming effective privacy restoration. We provide convergence guarantees showing that the Krylov approximation error decreases as O((k ^1/2-1)/(k^1/2+1)) where k is the Hessian condition number. The causal weighting mechanism ensures surgical updates, where only clients holding deleted data are modified, preserving model quality for unaffected participants and avoiding the instability of gradient-based approaches in asynchronous federated settings. This design provides interpretability as each update is directly traceable to the influence of the deleted data. The method's efficiency and precision make it suitable for production federated systems where deletion requests arrive asynchronously and computational budgets are constrained.

</details>


### [91] [Symmetrization of Loss Functions for Robust Training of Neural Networks in the Presence of Noisy Labels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20347)
*Alexandre Lemire Paquin,Brahim Chaib-Draa,Philippe Giguère*

TL;DR: 本文研究了针对多分类噪声标签问题的稳健损失函数，通过分解理论推导出了多分类无铰链损失，并构建了性能优异且平滑可控的新型损失函数（SGCE与α-MAE）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实际机器学习任务中，标注数据集成本高昂且易出错，因此亟需研究对标签噪声具有鲁棒性的损失函数。现有的研究主要集中在二分类场景，缺乏针对多分类场景下满足对称性条件的理论框架与稳健损失函数的有效构建。

Method: 利用多分类损失函数向对称分量与类无关项的唯一分解，推导出满足对称性条件的线性多分类无铰链损失函数；通过引入插值参数，构建了SGCE和α-MAE损失函数，在平衡鲁棒性与平滑度的同时，通过标准噪声标签数据集进行了实证评估。

Result: 从理论上证明了多分类无铰链损失是唯一的凸多分类对称损失，且是任意对称损失在相等得分向量附近的线性近似；实验结果表明，所提出的SGCE和α-MAE在多个标准噪声标签基准测试中展现出极具竞争力的性能。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了多分类环境下稳健损失函数的构建框架，证明了多分类无铰链（Un-hinged）损失在凸对称损失函数中的唯一性及其局部特性，并以此为基础构建了具有良好性能的插值损失函数（SGCE和α-MAE），为处理噪声标签问题提供了更灵活且稳健的工具。

Abstract: Labeling a training set is often expensive and susceptible to errors, making the design of robust loss functions for label noise an important problem. The symmetry condition provides theoretical guarantees for robustness to such noise. In this work, we study a symmetrization method arising from the unique decomposition of any multi-class loss function into a symmetric component and a class-insensitive term. In particular, symmetrizing the cross-entropy loss leads to a linear multi-class extension of the unhinged loss. Unlike in the binary case, the multi-class version must have specific coefficients in order to satisfy the symmetry condition. Under suitable assumptions, we show that this multi-class unhinged loss is the unique convex multi-class symmetric loss. We also show that it has a fundamental local role: the linear approximation of any symmetric loss around score vectors with equal components is equivalent to the multi-class unhinged loss. We then introduce SGCE and alpha-MAE, two loss functions that interpolate between the multi-class unhinged loss and the Mean Absolute Error while allowing control of the beta-smoothness of the loss. Experiments on standard noisy-label benchmarks show competitive performance compared with existing robust loss functions.

</details>


### [92] [Consistently Informative Soft-Label Temperature for Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20357)
*Hoang-Chau Luong,Nghia Van Vo,Kaiqi Zhao,Lingwei Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对传统知识蒸馏中全局固定温度导致软标签信息熵不一致的问题，本文提出 CIST 方法，通过样本自适应的温度调节与重加权机制，实现了更优的知识迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的知识蒸馏使用固定的全局温度，忽略了不同样本在逻辑值尺度和学习难度上的差异，导致教师软标签的熵表现不一致（有的过于尖锐，有的过于平滑），且教师与学生模型共享温度限制了学习效果。

Method: 提出了 CIST（一致性信息软标签温度）方法：1. 为教师和学生模型分配独立的样本级自适应温度，以确保教师软标签的信息量并放宽对逻辑值尺度（logit-scale）的严格匹配要求；2. 根据教师置信度和学生学习难度对蒸馏目标进行重新加权；3. 基于教师逻辑值最大值与温度的比率来动态调整温度，以控制输出分布的熵。

Result: 实验结果表明，CIST 在计算机视觉和自然语言处理任务中均优于标准知识蒸馏及其他强基线模型，且计算开销可忽略不计。

Conclusion: CIST 通过引入样本自适应的温度调节机制，克服了传统知识蒸馏中固定温度导致的软标签熵不一致问题，实现了更有效的知识迁移，且具有良好的通用性和极低的额外计算开销。

Abstract: Knowledge distillation (KD) transfers knowledge from a high-capacity teacher to a compact student by matching their predictive distributions, with temperature scaling serving as a central mechanism for smoothing teacher predictions and exposing informative "dark knowledge" beyond the hard label. However, the standard fixed-temperature design is inherently sample-agnostic. Since samples differ in logit scale and learning difficulty, a single global temperature produces teacher soft labels with highly inconsistent entropy: some predictions remain overly sharp and provide limited inter-class information, whereas others become over-smoothed and lose class-discriminative information. Moreover, sharing the same temperature between teacher and student further imposes rigid logit-scale alignment despite their capacity mismatch. To address these limitations, we propose CIST (Consistently Informative Soft-label Temperature), which assigns separate sample-wise adaptive temperatures to the teacher and student. This design produces consistently informative teacher soft labels while relaxing rigid teacher--student logit-scale matching. It also reweights the distillation objective according to teacher confidence and student learning difficulty. Theoretically, we show that teacher-label entropy is largely governed by the ratio between the maximum teacher logit and the temperature, providing a principled basis for adaptive smoothing. Empirically, CIST mitigates the inconsistency induced by fixed temperature, and experiments on both vision and language distillation tasks show consistent improvements over standard KD and strong baselines with negligible computational overhead.

</details>


### [93] [Nonlocal operator learning for fMRI encoding and decoding tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20389)

Abstract: Functional MRI data exhibit high-dimensional spatiotemporal structure, making both prediction and decoding challenging. In this work, we investigate neural integral-operator-based models for encoding and decoding tasks in fMRI, with particular emphasis on the role of nonlocal spatiotemporal context. We implement a latent neural integral operator framework that performs fixed point iterations in an auxiliary space from which classification and stimuli prediction is performed via a decoder. We evaluate our model on two open-source fMRI datasets.
  Our experiments examine both decoding of stimuli from fMRI recordings and encoding of fMRI dynamics from stimulus representations. A main focus is the effect of spatiotemporal context: we systematically compare short and long temporal windows, as well as the use of visual cortex vs whole brain recordings, and analyze their influence on performance and latent-space geometry. Across tasks and datasets, larger temporal windows generally improve results and produce more structured learned representations. In decoding experiments, the learned latent space often provides clearer class separation than the raw data. In encoding experiments, although absolute performance remains moderate due to the difficulty of the task, longer temporal windows still yield consistent gains.
  These findings suggest that neural integral operators provide a promising framework for modeling fMRI dynamics and that broader spatiotemporal context can be beneficial for both prediction and representation learning. More broadly, the results indicate that exploiting distributed nonlocal structure in brain dynamics requires model architectures specifically designed to capture such dependencies.

Abstract: Identifying latent variables and the causal structure involving them is essential across various scientific fields. While many existing works fall under the category of constraint-based methods (with e.g. conditional independence or rank deficiency tests), they may face empirical challenges such as testing-order dependency, error propagation, and choosing an appropriate significance level. These issues can potentially be mitigated by properly designed score-based methods, such as Greedy Equivalence Search (GES) (Chickering, 2002) in the specific setting without latent variables. Yet, formulating score-based methods with latent variables is highly challenging. In this work, we develop score-based methods that are capable of identifying causal structures containing causally-related latent variables with identifiability guarantees. Specifically, we show that a properly formulated scoring function can achieve score equivalence and consistency for structure learning of latent variable causal models. We further provide a characterization of the degrees of freedom for the marginal over the observed variables under multiple structural assumptions considered in the literature, and accordingly develop both exact and continuous score-based methods. This offers a unified view of several existing constraint-based methods with different structural assumptions. Experimental results validate the effectiveness of the proposed methods.

### [95] [Decomposing MXFP4 quantization error for LLM reinforcement learning: reducible bias, recoverable deadzone, and an irreducible floor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20402)
*Xiaocan Li,Shiliang Wu,Zheng Shen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对MXFP4量化在LLM强化学习训练中导致的精度损失，该论文揭示了量化误差的三重机制，并提出了相应的修正方案，成功在保持高效率的同时将模型精度恢复至接近BF16的水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MXFP4算术虽然能显著加速大语言模型的强化学习（RL）后训练，但量化带来的误差会导致严重的准确性下降。现有研究将量化误差视为单一噪声，缺乏对量化误差破坏训练的具体机制的深入分析。因此，本研究旨在深入解析量化误差的组成及其对RL训练过程的影响，以寻求恢复模型精度的方法。

Method: 该研究通过理论证明将MXFP4量化误差分解为“尺度偏差”（Scale bias）、“死区截断”（Deadzone truncation）和“网格噪声”（Grid noise）三个部分。针对这三种机制对应的RL失效模式，提出了组合修正策略：利用宏块缩放减少尺度偏差，采用异常值回退恢复被截断的微小值，并引入自适应量化噪声（AQN）调节策略熵。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-3B密集模型和Qwen3-30B-A3B混合专家模型上的实验表明，该研究提出的针对性修正策略能将量化模型的精度恢复至接近BF16的水平，性能差距分别控制在0.7%和3.0%以内。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了MXFP4量化误差的三重机制及其对RL训练中不同路径的破坏作用。通过针对性的修正方案（宏块缩放、异常值回退和自适应量化噪声），可以在维持模型性能的前提下，有效解决低精度量化带来的准确性下降问题，为大模型在RL场景下的高效低精度部署提供了理论依据与实践方案。

Abstract: MXFP4 arithmetic can dramatically accelerate reinforcement learning (RL) post-training of large language models (LLMs), yet the quantization error introduces severe accuracy degradation. Existing work treats the quantization error as a monolithic noise term, missing the distinct mechanisms upon interpreting how quantization error damages training. We prove an exact three-way decomposition of quantization error and show how each component dominates a distinct RL training pathway. Our theoretical and empirical analysis decomposes the MXFP4 quantization error into three additive components: "scale bias" from power-of-two rounding, "deadzone truncation" from zeroing small values, and "grid noise" from rounding to the nearest 4-bit grid. Each component dominates a distinct RL failure mode: scale bias accumulates multiplicatively through the backward pass, affecting gradient accuracy; deadzone truncation degrades rollout quality; and grid noise raises the policy's entropy. We combine corrections that are RL failure mode-targeted but not component-exclusive: Macro-block scaling to reduce scale bias, Outlier Fallback recovers deadzone entries, but also partially reduces scale bias induced error, and Adaptive Quantization Noise (AQN) for controlling the policy entropy. On Qwen2.5-3B dense and Qwen3-30B-A3B-Base mixture-of-experts model, the targeted corrections recover BF16 accuracy to within 0.7% and 3.0% respectively.

### [96] [Spectral Souping: A Unified Framework for Online Preference Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20408)
*Yinlam Chow,Guy Tennenholtz,Ted Yun,James Harrison,Arthur Gretton,Andre Barreto,Bo Dai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 RLHF 难以处理个体化差异的问题，本文提出了 Spectral Souping 框架，利用模型内部的通用谱表示，通过在推理时动态合并专门化策略，实现了高效的个性化偏好对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）通常只能将模型与人类的总体偏好对齐，难以满足不同个体用户之间多元化且往往相互冲突的偏好需求。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Spectral Souping”的框架：1. 离线阶段：训练一组专门针对不同细粒度偏好维度的策略基底（basis of specialized policies）；2. 在线阶段：通过在线适配算法，在推理时通过对这些策略进行参数合并（parameter merging）或输出合并，实现快速的个性化对齐。

Result: 实验结果表明，Spectral Souping 在在线偏好对齐基准测试中优于现有的先进方法，证明了其在无需昂贵在线训练的前提下，能够高效地将大语言模型动态适配到个体用户偏好。

Conclusion: Spectral Souping 提供了一种高效、可扩展且无需在线训练的策略，通过利用模型内部的谱表示特性，实现了大语言模型对个体用户偏好的动态适配，克服了传统 RLHF 在处理多元化需求时的局限性。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) effectively aligns Large Language Models (LLMs) with aggregate human preferences but often fails to address the diverse and conflicting needs of individual users. To overcome this issue, we introduce Spectral Souping, a unified framework for efficient, online preference alignment. Our contribution is the discovery of a universal spectral representation within LLMs, which is proven to be highly amenable to model merging. This theoretical insight enables a two-phase methodology: we first learn a basis of specialized policies offline, each focused on a distinct, fine-grained preference dimension. An online adaptation algorithm then efficiently ``soups'' these policies at inference time, either by merging their outputs or parameters, enabling rapid model adaptation without the need for costly online retraining w.r.t. tailored preference rewards. Experiments on online preference alignment benchmarks demonstrate that our method achieves significant performance improvements over existing state-of-the-art approaches, presenting a scalable and computationally efficient solution for dynamically adapting LLMs to individual user preferences.

### [97] [Supervised Latent Restructuring for Small-Data Quantum Learning in Plant Phenomics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20413)
*Alakananda Mitra,David H. Fleisher,Vangimalla Reddy,Chittaranjan Ray*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对小样本高维生物数据，本文提出了一种结合LDA重构与量子核对齐的混合工作流，探讨了数据压缩对表征几何及后续量子/经典模型分类性能的权衡关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维生物数据、极小样本量的场景下，传统核方法因难以提取有效的类别分离结构而失效。本文旨在探索如何通过压缩与重构技术优化数据表示，并评估其对下游量子核学习性能的影响。

Method: 本文提出了一种针对植物表型数据的混合分类工作流：首先将1280维深度图像嵌入压缩至64维（PCA），随后利用线性判别分析（LDA）将其重构为11维的监督潜在空间，最后在NVIDIA L40S硬件上应用GPU加速的量子核对齐（QKA）技术进行分类评估。

Result: 研究发现，监督学习下的LDA重构显著提升了数据的几何可分性（Silhouette系数从负值提升至0.197）；在下游评估中，线性模型（SVM/XGBoost）性能提升，但非线性模型（RBF-SVM/随机森林）性能因信息瓶颈而下降；此外，在受限优化预算下，QKA在重构后的空间中仍面临极大的训练挑战。

Conclusion: 论文得出结论：在小样本高维生物数据环境下，表征的几何结构是量子学习设计的核心变量。过度压缩虽然能改善线性判别能力，但会损失下游非线性模型所需的复杂特征，且单纯优化潜在空间几何结构并不足以直接保证量子核方法的性能，量子计算在处理此类受限压缩数据时仍面临严峻挑战。

Abstract: High-dimensional biological data often exhibit a severe mismatch between feature dimensionality and sample size, making reliable classification difficult in extremely small-data regimes. In these settings, kernel methods can lose discriminative power when latent compression fails to preserve class-separating structure. We study this problem in fine-grained plant phenomics and propose a hybrid workflow that compresses 1280-dimensional deep image embeddings into a 64-dimensional PCA space and then restructures them into an 11-dimensional supervised latent space using Linear Discriminant Analysis (LDA), followed by GPU-accelerated Quantum Kernel Alignment (QKA) on NVIDIA L40S hardware. Empirically, supervised latent restructuring substantially improves the geometric separability of the compressed representation, increasing the Silhouette coefficient from 0.003 in the raw embedding space and -0.006 in PCA-64 to 0.197 in the supervised LDA-11 space. However, downstream classical evaluation reveals a clear compression trade-off: Linear SVM and XGBoost improve in the restructured latent space, whereas RBF-SVM and Random Forest degrade under the same 11-dimensional bottleneck. Under a constrained optimization budget, QKA in this regime remains challenging, indicating that latent geometry alone is not sufficient for strong trainable quantum performance. These findings position representation geometry as a central design variable in small-data quantum learning and expose the practical difficulty of recovering nonlinear discriminative structure from aggressively compressed biological representations.

### [98] [Miller-Index-Based Latent Crystallographic Fracture Plane Reasoning with Vision-Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20416)

Conclusion: 研究表明，只要明确领域适用范围，多模态大语言模型（MLLM）能够作为基于结构化潜在先验的物理感知推理系统。该模型不仅能在理想条件下进行准确的潜在推理，还能在物理逻辑不成立时果断拒绝使用该潜在表示。

Abstract: We study whether multimodal large language models (MLLMs) can leverage crystallographic plane indices (Miller indices) as a structured latent representation for reasoning about fracture geometry. We formulate Miller indices $z = (h,k,l)$ as a latent variable governing idealized planar fracture and evaluate two complementary capabilities: (i) latent inference, where the model maps visual observations to plane hypotheses under physically valid conditions, and (ii) latent applicability assessment, where the model determines whether such a representation is meaningful for a given fracture image.
  Through extensive experiments spanning synthetic data, controlled 2D--3D geometric pairs, and real-world fracture images across multiple material classes -- including ceramics, glass, metals, and concrete -- we show that MLLMs can reliably perform latent inference in idealized settings and, critically, can reject the latent representation when the underlying physics does not support it. These results suggest that MLLMs can act as physics-aware reasoning systems conditioned on structured latent priors, provided that the domain of validity is explicitly modeled.

</details>


### [99] [Can Conversational XAI Improve User Performance? An Experimental Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20439)
*Sven Kruschel,Julian Rosenberger,Lasse Bohlen,Mathias Kraus,Patrick Zschech*

Method: 研究设计了一项受控实验，采用“设计即解释”（explainable-by-design）的预测模型，创建用户可以通过识别并补偿模型系统性错误来超越模型的任务环境。实验比较了两种辅助方式：对话式助手（conversational assistance）与问答式助手（Q&A-based assistance），通过预测准确率、模型理解度和错误识别率来评估用户表现。

Result: 在对42名参与者的初步测试中，所有实验组的参与者在性能上均显著超过了预测模型本身；然而，两种辅助方式在用户表现上没有显著差异，且整体用户参与度较为一般。

Abstract: Explainable AI (XAI) techniques aim to provide insights into predictive models and enhance user performance, yet they often fall short of these expectations. Conversational XAI assistants promise to overcome such limitations, but empirical evidence on their impact on objective performance measures remains limited. We propose an experimental design for evaluating explanation assistance through prediction accuracy, model understanding, and error identification. Using an explainable-by-design prediction model, we create conditions where users can outperform the model by identifying and compensating for systematic errors. We compare conversational assistance against Q&A-based assistance to assess which better supports users in working with model explanations. Preliminary results from testing our experimental design show that participants (N=42) in both treatments significantly outperformed the model but reveal no performance differences between assistance types and modest engagement overall. These findings inform refinements for our planned full study, including enhanced engagement interventions and investigation of the mechanisms driving improved predictions.

### [100] [LLM Pretraining Shapes a Generalizable Manifold: Insights into Cross-Modal Transfer to Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20449)
*Alexis Roger,Prateek Humane,Zhenghan Tai,Gwen Legate,Andrei Mircea,Vasilii Feofanov,Irina Rish*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了语言大模型在时间序列预测中的“跨模态迁移”奥秘：语言预训练预先构建了一个可重用的特征流形，而微调只需将时间序列动态映射到该流形中，从而证明了基础模型中已隐含了处理时间序列的结构化知识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究为什么语言预训练的Transformer模型能够有效地迁移到时间序列预测任务，并从理论和几何角度阐明跨模态迁移背后的内在机理。

Method: 作者通过线性探测（Linear Probing）评估冻结的大模型状态，分析预训练模型中的流形结构；利用检索机制验证隐含的动态特性；并通过分析梯度动力学、损失景观的各向异性以及微调参数的低秩特性（Low-rank updates）来揭示模型迁移的机制。

Result: 研究发现：1. 冻结的LLM状态无需成对监督即可解码出逼真的时间序列；2. 预训练初始化能产生更连贯的梯度和各向异性更强的损失景观；3. 微调本质上是低维对齐过程，模型重用了周期性、趋势性和重复性等预存特征，而非从头学习。

Conclusion: 本文提出了语言大模型在时间序列预测中表现出色的几何解释：语言预训练构建了一个通用的特征流形，而微调过程则是将数值动态投影到这些预定义的方向上，通过低秩更新实现高效学习。

Abstract: Can language-pretrained transformers become effective time-series forecasters, and why? In this paper, we show that cross-modal transfer arises because language pretraining preconditions time series training with a reusable manifold. A linear probe on frozen LLM states decodes realistic time-series trajectories without paired supervision, and retrieval in this projected space yields competitive forecasts, showing that structure and dynamics exist before finetuning. Pretrained initialization also improves optimization, producing coherent gradients and a highly anisotropic loss landscape unlike random initialization. Finetuning then acts as low-dimensional alignment, reusing existing directions rather than learning temporal primitives from scratch, as evidenced by low-rank updates, subspace alignment, and shared features for periodicity, trend, and repetition. Together, these results support a geometric account of LLM-to-time-series transfer: language pretraining builds the manifold, and finetuning projects numerical dynamics onto task-relevant directions.

### [101] [CASCADE Conformal Prediction: Uncertainty-Adaptive Prediction Intervals for Two-Stage Clinical Decision Support](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20468)
*Ricardo Diaz-Rincon,Muxuan Liang,Adolfo Ramirez-Zamora,Benjamin Shickel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 CASCADE 的新型共形预测框架，通过利用药物调整分类任务中的认知不确定性，实现了对帕金森病药物剂量预测区间的动态自适应缩放，在提升预测效率的同时增强了临床决策的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 帕金森病患者对药物反应差异大，现有 AI 模型在预测每日左旋多巴等效剂量（LEDD）时，缺乏对预测可靠性的有效量化，无法区分高置信度与低置信度决策，导致临床应用受限。

Method: 提出 CASCADE（通过共形与分布估计进行的校准自适应缩放）框架。该方法利用筛选分类器（判断是否需要调整药物）产生认知不确定性，并通过 Venn-Abers 多概率校准将此不确定性直接映射为回归任务的非一致性分数，从而动态缩放剂量预测的区间。

Result: 实验表明，与标准共形预测基准相比，CASCADE 在高置信度患者上的预测区间平均缩窄了 38.9%，同时在不确定病例中能够自动扩展区间，确保了预测的鲁棒性与覆盖率。

Conclusion: CASCADE 框架通过有效整合认知不确定性与预测区间，成功架起了帕金森病临床离散决策与连续剂量预测之间的桥梁，在保证覆盖率的同时显著提升了高置信度预测的精度。

Abstract: Effective medication management in Parkinson's Disease (PD) is challenging due to heterogeneous disease progression, variable patient response, and medication side effects. While AI models can forecast levodopa equivalent daily dose (LEDD) as a measure of medication needs, standard uncertainty quantification often fails to communicate the reliability of these predictions, treating high and low confidence clinical decisions identically. We introduce CASCADE (Calibrated Adaptive Scaling via Conformal And Distributional Estimation), a novel conformal prediction framework that propagates epistemic uncertainty from a screening classifier to adapt downstream predictions. Unlike standard conformal methods that rely on auxiliary residual regression, we leverage epistemic uncertainty from a primary classification task (identifying whether a medication change is needed) to dynamically scale the prediction intervals of a secondary regression task (predicting how much change). By mapping Venn-Abers multi-probabilistic uncertainty directly to non-conformity scores, our framework achieves continuous risk adaptation. We demonstrate that this ``cascade effect'' produces highly efficient intervals for confident patients (38.9% narrower than standard conformal baselines) while automatically expanding intervals to ensure robust coverage for uncertain cases, bridging the gap between discrete clinical decision-making and continuous dose forecasting in PD.

### [102] [Training Language Agents to Learn from Experience](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20477)
*Yuval Shalev,Zifeng Ding,Mateja Jamnik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了上下文训练（ICT）框架和MetaGym库，通过强化学习训练智能体将过往经验转化为可提升未来任务表现的通用提示，成功实现了语言智能体的跨任务自我改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于反射（Reflection）的方法通常仅限于在单个任务实例内进行自我修正，无法将宝贵的经验提炼为可重用的“经验教训”以提升处理未来未知任务的能力。研究旨在探究语言智能体是否能实现跨任务的自我改进，即“学会如何学习”。

Method: 1. 提出了上下文训练（ICT）任务框架，用于评估跨任务的自我改进能力。
2. 引入了“反射器-执行者”（Reflector-Actor）架构，反射器通过观察执行者的轨迹，生成优化后的系统提示。
3. 设计了一套基于强化学习（RL）的训练流水线，使反射器能够直接从经验中学习生成提示，无需人类标注示例。
4. 开发了MetaGym库，用于构建元环境，支持此类自我改进智能体的后续研究。

Result: 在ALFWorld和MiniHack等基准测试中，经过训练的反射器在大多数未见任务族群上均优于未经训练的基线模型，验证了通过经验学习改进智能体能力的可行性。在某些情况下，模型表现出了跨越不同环境的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了语言智能体通过经验学习（即“学会如何学习”）是可行的。通过上下文训练（ICT）框架，智能体能够将特定任务的经验内化为可重用的通用系统提示，从而显著提升在未见任务中的表现，为构建自主进化型智能体提供了重要范式。

Abstract: Language agents can adapt from experience in interactive environments, but current reflection-based methods can only self-correct within a single task instance. Whether such experience can be distilled into reusable lessons that improve performance on future unseen tasks remains unclear. We address this problem by introducing the In-context Training (ICT) task, a framework for evaluating cross-task self-improvement in language agents. In ICT, a reflector model observes trajectories collected by an actor model and generates system prompts intended to improve the actor's performance on future unseen tasks. We then propose an RL-based training pipeline for learning such reflections directly from experience, without human-provided examples. Across ALFWorld and MiniHack, our trained reflectors outperform an untrained baseline on most held-out task families, showing that the ability to learn from experience can itself be learned. In some cases, we observe generalisation beyond the benchmark on which the reflector was trained, to substantially different environments. Finally, we introduce MetaGym, a generic Python library for constructing meta-environments, enabling future research on self-improving language agents.

### [103] [ZEBRA: Zero-shot Budgeted Resource Allocation for LLM Orchestration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20485)
*May Hamri,Inbal Talgam-Cohen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ZEBRA是一种零样本预算分配框架，通过数学优化（非线性背包问题求解）动态分配多智能体流水线的计算预算，在显著提升资源利用效率的同时，实现了优于大模型直接判断的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着自主智能体执行复杂端到端任务，核心痛点已从“如何遵守预算”转向“如何高效利用有限预算”。现有方法多局限于单智能体内部的步骤控制或基于RL的资源分配，缺乏针对多智能体流水线推理阶段的预算动态切分机制。

Method: 提出ZEBRA框架，将多阶段预算分配问题转化为连续非线性背包问题。首先利用LLM控制器估计各阶段的效用曲线，随后通过拉格朗日乘子法的“注水算法（water-filling search）”计算最优预算分配比例，并支持加法和乘法两种效用聚合方式。

Result: 在APPS编程基准测试中，当预算为无约束花费的50%时，ZEBRA恢复了94.4%的性能，显著优于传统的LLM直接分配法（88.1%）。在HotpotQA三阶段任务中，ZEBRA表现出对流水线结构的自适应性，性能提升了14.3个百分点，且对效用曲线估计的噪声具有稳健性。

Conclusion: ZEBRA证明了在推理时引入轻量级的算法指导，能够有效提升自主多智能体系统在预算约束下的资源分配效率与决策质量。该方法通过将预算分配问题形式化为数学规划问题，实现了跨任务和跨场景的稳健适应性。

Abstract: As autonomous agents increasingly execute end-to-end tasks under fixed monetary budgets, the pressing open question shifts from whether the budget is respected, to how to spend it effectively. Existing budget-aware methods typically control reasoning step-by-step within a single agent, or learn resource allocation policies via RL. None address how to split a budget across the composing phases of a multi-agent pipeline at inference time. We propose ZEBRA, a zero-shot framework that reduces multi-phase budget allocation to a continuous nonlinear knapsack problem: an LLM controller estimates per-phase utility curves, and a water-filling search on the Lagrange multiplier returns the per-phase split. Additive and multiplicative aggregations are unified under the same solver. On a $150$-task APPS coding benchmark, both ZEBRA variants outperform LLM-direct (budget allocation directly by an LLM) on every aggregate metric. At a budget of $α= 0.5$ of the unconstrained spend, ZEBRA recovers $94.4\%$ of unconstrained quality, versus $88.1\%$ for LLM-direct. The advantage is statistically significant and transfers beyond coding: on a $3$-phase HotpotQA pipeline, ZEBRA beats LLM-direct by $14.3$pp, with allocations empirically robust to curve-estimation noise. On HotpotQA, ZEBRA arrives at a different budget split (near-balanced) compared to the APPS one (skewed towards a refinement phase), showing adaptation to the pipeline structure. More broadly, we show that lightweight algorithmic guidance at inference time can improve the economic behavior of autonomous multi-agent systems.

</details>


### [104] [Tippett-minimum Fusion of Representation-space Diffusion Models for Multi-Encoder Out-of-Distribution Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20502)
*Neelkamal Bhuyan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为EncMin2L的框架，通过多编码器协同与扩散模型，在无需OOD标签的前提下，以极高的效率和精度统一解决了多种不同类型的分布偏移（OOD）检测难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的OOD检测方法往往难以同时应对多种类型的分布偏移（如领域变化、语义差异、纹理变化及协变量损坏）。此外，现有的多编码器方法通常计算成本高昂，且缺乏针对不同偏移类型的专项优化。因此，需要一种高效、无需OOD标签且能综合多维度特征的检测框架。

Method: 本文提出了EncMin2L（一种编码器无关的两级最小化门控机制）。首先，利用ID数据训练多个编码器，并通过η²（类条件F检验）和Δμ（合成扰动下的对数似然偏移）两个指标量化编码器对不同偏移类型的敏感度；其次，采用表示空间扩散模型（RDM）作为似然估计器；最后，利用Tippett最小p值法聚合各编码器的评分，并通过两级min(·)门控进行校准。

Result: EncMin2L在所有四种类型的分布偏移任务中均实现了≥0.94的AUROC，在多个重叠基准测试中超越了当前的先进水平（SOTA），同时参数量比单一结构的集成基线模型降低了2.3倍。

Conclusion: 本文提出的EncMin2L框架通过结合多编码器的互补优势，成功在无需OOD标签的情况下实现了对多种分布偏移类型的统一检测。该方法不仅在性能上超越了现有先进的OOD检测器，而且在计算效率和参数规模上具备显著优势，为鲁棒的异常检测提供了新的范式。

Abstract: We address out-of-distribution (OOD) detection across the full spectrum of distribution shifts -- global domain changes, semantic divergence, texture differences, and covariate corruptions -- through a multi-encoder fusion of per-encoder representation-space diffusion models (RDMs). We statistically identify each encoder's sensitivity to specific shift types from ID data alone and introduce EncMin2L -- an encoder-agnostic two-level $\min(\cdot)$-gate that combines and calibrates per-encoder diffusion-based likelihood detectors without OOD labels, outperforming monolithic multi-encoder baselines at $2.3\times$ lower parameter cost. Two ID-data diagnostics: $η^2$ (class-conditional F-test) and $Δμ$ (log-likelihood shift under synthetic corruptions) -- quantify encoder specialization, while a Tippett minimum $p$-value combination aggregates per-encoder scores into a single, calibration-stable OOD signal. EncMin2L achieves $\geq 0.94$ AUROC across all four shift types simultaneously, outperforming the state-of-the-art representation-space diffusion OOD detectors across overlapping benchmarks.

### [105] [Reinforcing Human Behavior Simulation via Verbal Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20506)
*Weiwei Sun,Xuhui Zhou,Jiarui Liu,Weihua Du,Haojia Sun,Yiqing Xie,Qianou Ma,Sihao Chen,Mengting Wan,Longqi Yang,Pei Zhou,Sherry Wu,Sean Welleck,Graham Neubig,Yiming Yang,Maarten Sap*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型在社会行为模拟方面的不足，本文提出了 DITTO 框架，通过将语言反馈直接整合进强化学习训练流程，成功实现了对模型行为的精准调优，并在涵盖人类社会交互的 SOUL 基准测试中展现了超越现有强基准模型（如 GPT-5.4）的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了 DITTO 框架，通过在强化学习流程中引入语言反馈，利用 GRPO（Group Relative Policy Optimization）联合优化原始输出和经反馈改进后的输出。此外，作者还构建了 SOUL 基准测试集，涵盖心理理论、角色扮演、社交技能等 10 项任务，用于评估模型的人类行为模拟能力。

Result: DITTO 在 SOUL 基准测试中取得了显著成效，平均性能比基准模型提升了 36%，并在 10 项任务中的 6 项表现优于 GPT-5.4，证明了该方法在处理人类行为模拟任务上的优越性。

Conclusion: DITTO 证明了将语言反馈视为强化学习中的一等信号，是训练大语言模型以实现人类行为模拟的一种高效且具有前景的途径。通过将口头指导蒸馏到基准策略中，该方法不仅提升了模型性能，还克服了传统标量奖励函数在复杂社会行为模拟中的局限性。

Abstract: Humans learn social norms and behaviors from verbal feedback (e.g., a parent saying "that was rude" or a friend explaining "here's why that hurt"). Yet, learning from feedback for LLMs has largely focused on domains like code and math, where RL rewards are directly verifiable and condensed into scalar values. As LLMs are increasingly used to simulate human behavior, e.g., standing in for users, patients, students, and other personas, there is a pressing need to make them more human-like, which requires embracing a fundamentally different kind of signal: feedback that is verbal, subjective, and multi-faceted. We present DITTO, a model trained by treating verbal feedback as a first-class signal in reinforcement learning. After each rollout, DITTO receives verbal feedback and generates a feedback-conditioned improved rollout; both outputs are jointly optimized with GRPO, distilling verbal guidance into the base policy without requiring feedback at test time. We also introduce SOUL (Simulation gym Of hUman-Like behavior), a unified benchmark and training data suite spanning 10 tasks across six categories: Theory of Mind, character role play, social skill, learner simulation, user simulation, and persona simulation. DITTO achieves an average 36% improvement over the base model and exceeds GPT-5.4 on 6 of 10 SOUL benchmarks, demonstrating that RL with verbal feedback is a promising direction for training LLMs to simulate human behavior.

### [106] [Online Conformal Prediction with Corrupted Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20515)
*Bowen Wang,Matteo Zecchin,Osvaldo Simeone*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了反馈数据受损时在线共形预测（OCP）的性能下降问题，并提出了两种改进的鲁棒性OCP方案（滤波与主动补偿），实现了在反馈噪声干扰下的有效校准保证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代人工智能系统要求在在线和非平稳环境下具备可靠的不确定性估计，在线共形预测（OCP）是主流解决方案。然而，现有的OCP方法高度依赖于对过去预测覆盖情况的精确反馈，但在实际应用中，反馈数据常受到噪声、通信故障或对抗性攻击的污染，导致OCP的校准保证失效，因此迫切需要开发具有鲁棒性的在线共形预测方法。

Method: 本文首先量化分析了反馈污染对标准OCP误覆盖率的影响；随后提出了两种鲁棒性方案：一是基于阈值结构特征的“滤波”方法（Robust OCP via filtering），用于剔除可疑的反馈；二是引入“主动补偿”机制（Robust OCP via active compensation），通过调整更新步长来抵消反馈误差的影响。此外，作者还推导了在独立随机翻转和有界记忆误差模型下的理论误覆盖保证。

Result: 实验结果表明，在反馈受到污染的情况下，本文提出的两种方法均能显著优于基准OCP方法。不仅大幅提升了模型的校准稳定性，还将预测集的大小保持在更小的水平，有效克服了传统方法在不可靠反馈环境下的局限性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过理论和实验证明，在反馈存在噪声或人为干扰的情况下，标准的在线共形预测（OCP）不再可靠。所提出的稳健OCP方案能够有效缓解反馈偏差，在维持预测集覆盖保证的同时，显著提升了模型在非平稳环境下的校准性能和实用性。

Abstract: Modern artificial intelligence systems require calibrated uncertainty estimates that remain reliable in sequential and non-stationary environments. Online conformal prediction (OCP) addresses this challenge through adaptively updated prediction sets that provide deterministic long-run miscoverage guarantees. These guarantees, however, hinge on the assumption of perfect feedback about the coverage of past prediction sets. In practice, the observed miscoverage indicator may be corrupted by noise, communication failures, or adversarial manipulation, which can severely degrade OCP's calibration guarantees. In this paper, we study OCP under corrupted feedback. We first model feedback corruption as an arbitrary binary flip sequence, and analyze how feedback corruption affects and degrades the miscoverage performance of standard OCP. We then propose two robust schemes: robust OCP via filtering, which leverages the structural properties of the predicted threshold to filter corrupted feedback, and robust OCP via active compensation, which incorporates an active compensation mechanism to mitigate the effect of corrupted feedback. For both methods, we establish explicit miscoverage guarantees, which are further specialized for an independent stochastic flip model and for an arbitrary error model with memory bounds. Experiments on real-world datasets validate the proposed approach, showing markedly improved calibration and significantly smaller prediction sets compared with baseline OCP methods under corrupted feedback.

</details>


### [107] [An exponential mechanism based on quadratic approximations for fine-tuning machine learning models with privacy guarantees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20521)
*Hoang Tran,Jorge Ramirez,Jiayi Wang,Alberto Bocchinfuso,Christopher Stanley,M. Paul Laiu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于指数机制的差分隐私微调算法，通过局部二次近似和随机投影技术，在保护敏感数据集隐私的同时，实现了高效且高精度的模型微调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微调预训练模型到小型敏感数据集时，存在过拟合和记忆个体数据点的风险，可能导致隐私泄露。现有的差分隐私微调方法在精度与计算效率上仍有提升空间。

Method: 1. 构建了一个包含预训练模型局部二次近似与新数据集信息的效用函数；2. 利用指数机制进行采样，推导出了多元正态分布的闭式精确采样方法；3. 引入随机投影策略以降低高维模型下的计算复杂度。

Result: 1. 提供了完善的差分隐私保障、敏感度边界及准确性估计理论分析；2. 在MNIST和MIMIC数据集上的实验表明，该方法在隐私保护与模型精度之间取得了良好的平衡，性能优于现有的差分隐私微调技术。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于指数机制的差分隐私微调算法，通过构建局部二次近似的效用函数，实现了高维模型的高效且隐私保护的微调，在保证隐私的同时保持了模型在敏感数据集上的良好性能。

Abstract: Fine-tuning adapts a pretrained machine learning model to a small, sensitive dataset, but this process risks memorizing individual new data points, making the model vulnerable to adversaries who seek to extract sensitive information. In this work, we develop a randomized algorithm based on the exponential mechanism for fine-tuning while ensuring differential privacy. Our key idea is to construct a simple utility function that combines a local quadratic approximation of the pretrained model with information from the new dataset. The resulting exponential mechanism admits exact sampling from a multivariate normal distribution in closed form. We establish theoretical privacy guarantees, sensitivity bounds, and accuracy estimations for our method. We further introduce a random-projection strategy that makes the approach scalable to high-dimensional models. Numerical experiments on the MNIST benchmark and the MIMIC clinical dataset demonstrate competitive performance against existing differentially private fine-tuning techniques.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种名为 Ada2MS 的新型优化算法。该算法通过在元素级二阶矩估计（AdamW 的特点）和全局二阶矩估计（Momentum SGD 的特点）之间进行连续指数插值，实现了从 AdamW 类行为到 Momentum SGD 类行为的平滑过渡。

Abstract: Optimization algorithms are core methods by which machine learning models iteratively minimize loss functions, update parameters, learn from data, and improve performance. Momentum SGD and AdamW represent two important optimization paradigms. AdamW produces stable updates and usually has strong robustness across training scenarios, but its generalization performance is sometimes weaker than that of momentum methods. Momentum SGD can often obtain better generalization after careful tuning, but it is more sensitive to gradient-scale variation and hyperparameter settings. To balance the strengths and weaknesses of the two paradigms, this paper proposes Ada2MS, an optimization algorithm that achieves a smooth transition between AdamW-like behavior and momentum-SGD-like behavior through continuous exponential interpolation between elementwise second-moment estimates and global second-moment estimates. On the visual tasks evaluated in this study, Ada2MS obtains competitive results under a unified optimizer-comparison protocol. The code will be released at https://github.com/mengzhu0308/Ada2MS

*Lukas Billera,Hedwig Nora Nordlinder,Ben Murrell*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了“潜在过程生成匹配”（Latent Process Generator Matching）框架，将观察到的生成状态定义为可处理马尔可夫过程 $Y_t$ 的确定性映射 $X_t = \Phi(Y_t)$，并证明了可以在图像空间上学习一个具有与投影过程相同单时间边际分布的随机过程生成器。

Result: 该框架概括并涵盖了文献中现有的离散潜在过程结果，为扩散风格的生成模型在辅助状态下的学习提供了更广泛的理论支撑，并证明了在保持边际分布一致性的前提下，可以有效简化生成过程中的状态依赖。

Conclusion: 该研究通过提出潜在过程生成匹配框架，成功将生成匹配理论从静态潜在变量扩展到时间依赖的潜在条件过程，为理解和优化扩散模型及流匹配模型提供了统一的数学基础。

Abstract: Many recent flow-matching and diffusion-style generative models rely on auxiliary stochastic dynamics during training: a richer process is simulated to define conditional targets, but the auxiliary state is either intractable to sample at generation time or simply not part of the desired output. Existing Generator Matching theory formalises conditioning on static latent random variables, and several recent papers prove special cases of projection results for particular augmented-state constructions. We introduce latent process generator matching, a general framework that treats the observed generative state as a deterministic image $X_t=Φ(Y_t)$ of a tractable Markov process $Y_t$. We show that in this setting one may learn the generator of a stochastic process on the image space which has the same one-time marginal distributions as the projected process. This generalizes and subsumes the discrete latent process results from the literature, and extends Generator Matching from static latent variables to a rich family of time-dependent latent conditional processes.

### [112] [TriForces: Augmenting Atomistic GNNs for Transferable Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20581)

### [113] [ReversedQ: Opportunities for Faster Q-Learning in Episodic Online Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20592)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究指出，现有的无模型后验采样强化学习方法为了证明理论保证，往往依赖于过慢的学习过程。本文旨在识别并解决这些学习瓶颈，通过改进算法策略，实现更快速的探索与收敛。

Method: 本文在Wang等人提出的RandomizedQ框架基础上，通过三项改进构建了ReversedQ算法：(1) 优化价值函数的更新顺序；(2) 调整价值函数的更新频率；(3) 改进价值函数的初始化策略，从而解决了原有方法中存在的学习延迟问题。

Abstract: We study model-free Q-learning in finite-horizon episodic Markov Decision Processes (MDPs) with stationary dynamics across episodes. In particular, we identify three opportunities for faster learning - (i) value-function update order, (ii) update frequencies, and (iii) value-function initialization. ### [114] [Compositional Transduction with Latent Analogies for Offline Goal-Conditioned Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20609)
*Junseok Kim,Dohyeong Kim,Mineui Hong,Songhwai Oh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对离线目标条件强化学习中组合泛化能力不足的挑战，本文提出了一种基于类比转换的新方法，通过学习任务内源性表征，实现了在不同上下文组合下的高效泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的离线目标条件强化学习（GCRL）多依赖于轨迹拼接，难以处理多样的上下文变化。该研究旨在解决泛化能力不足的问题，通过组合任务内源性类比与特定上下文，实现对未见目标的有效达成。

Method: 研究形式化了“类比转换”（Analogy Transduction），通过构建专门的类比表征，捕捉最优任务执行中随上下文变化的不变性与变动性；并引入了一种新的离线强化学习方法，实现了在未见过的类比-上下文组合上的泛化。

Result: 在 OGBench 机器人操作环境中进行了实验，结果显示该方法在性能上显著优于现有的非类比转换方法，证明了其在处理未知任务组合时的强大泛化能力。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的类比转换方法通过解耦任务内源性和上下文变化，有效地解决了离线目标条件强化学习中组合泛化能力不足的问题，为处理未见过的情境组合提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Compositional generalization is essential for reaching unseen goals under novel contextual variations in offline goal-conditioned reinforcement learning (GCRL), where a generalist goal-reaching agent must be learned from limited data. Most prior approaches pursue this via trajectory stitching over temporally contiguous segments, which limits composing behaviors across varying contexts. To overcome this limitation, we formalize analogy transduction as synthesizing new plans by composing task-endogenous analogies with given contexts and propose a novel analogy representation tailored for it. Grounded in our theory, this analogy representation captures what changes under optimal task execution, remains invariant to contextual variations, and is sufficient for optimal goal reaching. We further contend that generalization to unseen analogy-context pairs is a practical obstacle in analogy transduction, and introduce a new approach for offline GCRL that enables analogy transduction beyond seen pairs to unseen combinations. We empirically demonstrate the effectiveness of our approach on OGBench manipulation environments, substantially outperforming prior methods that do not perform analogy transduction. Project page: https://rllab-snu.github.io/projects/CTA/

### [115] [Matryoshka Concept Bottleneck Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20612)
*Ziye Chen,Hongbin Lin,Xinyue Xu,Jie Li,Lijie Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了Matryoshka概念瓶颈模型（MCBM），通过嵌套概念结构优化，解决了传统可解释模型在专家人工干预时的高成本问题，实现了在单一模型中进行高效、动态的自适应概念推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的概念瓶颈模型（CBM）在实际部署中存在缺陷：由于需要专家对所有概念进行验证，测试时的人工干预成本极高。现有的解决方案（如固定概念集或训练多个特定模型）要么成本高昂，要么计算和维护负担过重，缺乏灵活性。

Method: 提出Matryoshka概念瓶颈模型（MCBM）。该方法受“俄罗斯套娃”表示学习启发，通过最大相关性和最小冗余度原则对概念进行嵌套排序。模型在训练时优化嵌套结构，允许在推理过程中根据不同的概念预算（concept budget）动态调整粒度，从而实现无需重训练即可在不同层次进行推断。

Result: 理论上，MCBM将预期的专家干预成本从线性复杂度 $O(K)$ 降低至对数复杂度 $O(\log K)$，并保证了性能随概念数量增加的单调性。实验结果表明，MCBM在保持与独立训练模型同等预测准确率的同时，实现了更高效、动态的专家交互支持。

Conclusion: 本文提出的Matryoshka概念瓶颈模型（MCBM）成功解决了传统CBM在测试时人工干预成本过高的问题。通过嵌套概念层次结构，该模型实现了在单一模型架构内进行多粒度推断，在维持高性能的同时，显著提升了专家干预的灵活性与效率。

Abstract: Concept Bottleneck Models (CBMs) have emerged as a prominent paradigm for interpretable deep learning, learning by grounding predictions in human-understandable concepts. However, their practical deployment is hindered by the high cost of test-time intervention, as correcting model errors typically requires human experts to manually inspect and verify a large set of predicted concepts. Existing approaches suffer from a fundamental structural limitation: they either adopt a single static concept set, forcing experts to exhaustively annotate concepts and incurring prohibitive intervention costs, or train multiple models tailored to different concept budgets, resulting in substantial computational and maintenance overhead. To address this challenge, we propose the Matryoshka Concept Bottleneck Model (MCBM), a unified architecture that enables adaptive concept utilization within a single model. Inspired by Matryoshka Representation Learning, MCBM organizes concepts into a nested hierarchy based on maximum relevance and minimum redundancy, allowing inference at multiple levels of conceptual granularity without retraining. Theoretically, we show that MCBM reduces the expected intervention costs from linear to logarithmic order, $O(\log K)$, while guaranteeing monotonic performance improvement. Empirically, extensive experiments demonstrate that MCBM matches the performance of independently trained models while enabling dynamic and efficient expert interaction.

### [116] [SURF: Steering the Scalarization Weight to Uniformly Traverse the Pareto Front](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20619)
*Liuyuan Jiang,Chentong Huang,Lisha Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多目标优化中权重采样导致的帕累托前沿（PF）分布不均匀问题，本文提出了 SURF 算法，通过对标量化路径进行几何分析并构建累积分布函数（CDF），实现了在帕累托前沿上的均匀采样，并在多项实验中证明了其优越性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多目标优化中，常用的标量化方法（Scalarization）简单且易扩展，但在实际应用中，均匀采样权重往往无法在帕累托前沿上实现均匀的覆盖。作者旨在通过几何手段量化并修正这一不匹配问题，从而生成能更好反映用户偏好的多样化解。

Method: 作者首先通过标量化路径的几何分析，定义了标量化权重与帕累托前沿（PF）覆盖速度之间的映射关系，并推导出了弧长累积分布函数（CDF）。基于此，作者提出了 SURF 方法：针对结构化问题推导闭式解，针对通用问题则采用迭代式 CDF 重构与权重重采样策略，从而在实现均匀覆盖的同时保证了收敛性。

Result: 理论分析表明，在特定条件下，SURF 算法能够线性收敛至有限的采样底限。实验部分通过多目标强盗问题（Bandits）、多目标强化学习环境以及大语言模型对齐任务验证了 SURF 的有效性，结果显示该方法在实现帕累托前沿均匀覆盖方面显著优于基准方法。

Conclusion: 该研究通过几何分析揭示了标量化权重与帕累托前沿分布之间的非线性映射关系，提出了一种具备通用性和普适性的采样方法 SURF。该方法能够有效解决多目标优化中权重采样分布不均匀的问题，在处理大规模或复杂模型（如大语言模型对齐）时表现出优异的均匀覆盖能力和计算效率。

Abstract: Scalarization is widely used in multi-objective optimization owing to its simplicity and scalability. In many applications, the goal is to generate solutions that represent diverse user preferences, ideally with uniform coverage of the Pareto front (PF). However, uniformly sampling scalarization weights usually induces non-uniform coverage of the PF. We explain this mismatch through a geometric analysis of the scalarization path. As the scalarization weight varies, the corresponding solutions trace the PF with a generally non-uniform traversal speed. This speed induces an arc-length cumulative distribution function (CDF); inverting this CDF map yields a principled rule for selecting weights that produce uniform PF coverage. Building on this insight, we propose SURF (Sampling Uniformly along the PaReto Front). For structured problems, including bi-objective bandits, we derive closed-form expressions for this CDF map and the resulting PF-aware weight sampling rule. For general problems, SURF alternates between CDF reconstruction and weight sampling. Theoretically, we show that under provable conditions, SURF converges linearly to an unavoidable finite-sampling floor. Empirically, experiments on bandits, multi-objective-gymnasium, and multi-objective LLM alignment demonstrate that SURF efficiently achieves more uniform PF coverage than baselines.

### [117] [Dynamic Shapley Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20620)
*Xuan Yang,Hsi-Wen Chen,Ming-Syan Chen,Jian Pei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 D-Shap，一种高效的动态数据价值评估框架。它将 Shapley 值计算视为动态矩阵维护问题，通过利用任务与数据的局部相关性，显著降低了数据和任务变更时的计算开销，实现了高效且高质量的数据贡献评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于 Shapley 的数据评估方法虽然理论严谨，但由于计算成本极高，无法满足任务和训练数据动态变化场景下的实时需求。现有方法通常将其视为一次性任务，缺乏重用机制，导致任何变动都需要全量重新计算。

Method: 1. 将 Shapley 值表示为“玩家-任务”矩阵，将动态更新转化为结构化矩阵维护问题。
2. 利用“效用局部性”和“联盟局部性”原理，通过结构感知插值进行任务更新。
3. 引入“自评估（self-valuation）”机制，基于训练数据构建初始矩阵，结合可扩展子集重用和覆盖感知锚点选择，无需预设评估任务。

Result: 实验表明，D-Shap 在多种模型上实现了毫秒级的任务更新，将玩家更新的计算成本降低了多达三个数量级，同时其评估质量与全量重新计算相当。

Conclusion: D-Shap 框架成功将 Shapley 值计算转化为高效的动态矩阵维护问题，通过利用数据与任务之间的局部性特征，在大幅降低计算复杂度的同时保证了评估质量，为动态场景下的数据价值评估提供了高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Shapley-based data valuation provides a principled way to quantify the contribution of training data, but its high computational cost makes it impractical in dynamic settings where tasks and training players evolve. Existing methods treat Shapley computation as a one-shot process and collapse contributions into aggregated scores, preventing reuse and requiring recomputation under any change. We introduce a new perspective that represents Shapley values as a player-by-task matrix and formulates dynamic valuation as a structured matrix maintenance problem. We exploit the fact that each task depends on a small subset of training players and that similar tasks yield similar valuations, leading to utility locality and coalition locality. Based on these insights, we propose D-Shap, a dynamic valuation framework that enables efficient updates by modifying only a small portion of the matrix: new task valuations are inferred via structure-aware interpolation, while updates induced by new players are confined to affected local matrix blocks. To eliminate the need for pre-specified evaluation tasks, we introduce self-valuation, which constructs the initial matrix directly from training data, supported by scalable subset reuse and coverage-aware anchor selection. Experiments across diverse models show that D-Shap performs task updates in milliseconds and reduces the cost of player updates by up to three orders of magnitude, while achieving valuation quality competitive with full recomputation.

</details>


### [118] [Same Target, Different Basins: Hard vs. Soft Labels for Annotator Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20642)
*Mirerfan Gheibi,Gashin Ghazizadeh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文探讨了在标注存在分歧时，使用“硬标签交付”策略（如多轮遍历或随机标签采样）替代传统的软标签训练，不仅在稀疏标注场景下表现更优，还能引导模型收敛到更平坦的解，提升泛化与OOD检测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标注者的不一致往往反映了认知上的不确定性，而非简单的标签噪声。现有的将投票折叠为单一标签或直接在经验软标签分布上训练的方法，可能无法有效利用这些不确定性信息，因此作者旨在探索“硬标签交付”作为一种替代方案。

Method: 研究对比了两种硬标签交付方法：1. 多轮遍历（Multipass）：在数据集大小固定的前提下，轮流使用观察到的标签；2. 随机标签采样（SLS）：在每个训练周期开始时为每个样本采样一个标签。研究还引入了确定性控制和洗牌式SLS作为对照实验，并从理论上证明了SLS与软标签交叉熵优化的是相同的预期目标。

Result: 在CIFAR-10H数据集上，当每个样本的标注较少时，硬标签交付优于软标签训练；当样本拥有完整标注分布时，两者效果持平。此外，硬标签交付方法倾向于收敛到更平坦的解，在SVHN和CIFAR-100的分布外（OOD）检测任务中表现出更好的稳健性。

Conclusion: “多轮遍历”（multipass）是处理原始标注计数的强有力的实践默认方案，而“随机标签采样”（SLS）在标注稀疏时表现出优势，且在标注充分时与软标签训练效果相当。研究表明，硬标签策略有助于模型收敛到更平坦的损失函数极小值区域，从而提升模型泛化能力。

Abstract: When annotators disagree, that disagreement can reflect epistemic uncertainty rather than simple label noise. We study hard-label delivery as an alternative to the usual choices of collapsing votes to a single label or training directly on the empirical soft-label distribution. We focus on two primary hard-label methods: multipass, which cycles through observed votes while keeping the dataset size fixed, and stochastic label sampling (SLS), which samples one label per example at the start of each epoch. On CIFAR-10H, we find that when only a small number of annotations per example is available, hard-label delivery improves over soft-label training, with larger improvements where the sparse empirical target is farther from the full annotator distribution. When full annotator distributions are available, both hard-label methods match soft-label training. We use deterministic control as an ablation of multipass and shuffled SLS as a control that breaks the example-to-distribution match. We also show that SLS and soft-label cross-entropy optimize the same expected objective. Hard-label delivery also converges to flatter basins, with supporting descriptive evidence from OOD detection on SVHN and CIFAR-100. Overall, these results suggest that multipass is a strong practical default when raw vote counts are available, while SLS offers a lightweight alternative that remains competitive when only a few votes per example are available and matches soft-label training when full annotator distributions are available.

</details>


### [119] [AVSD: Adaptive-View Self-Distillation by Balancing Consensus and Teacher-Specific Privileged Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20643)
*Duy Nguyen,Hanqi Xiao,Archiki Prasad,Zaid Khan,Anirban Das,Austin Zhang,Sambit Sahu,Hyunji Lee,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Mohit Bansal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 AVSD（自适应视图自蒸馏）的新方法，通过整合多种特权信息视图并分离跨视图共识与特权残差，显著提升了语言模型在数学和代码任务中的性能，解决了传统自蒸馏方法中的信息不对称和视图选择难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自蒸馏方法中，教师模型依赖于推理时学生无法获取的特权信息，这导致了信息不对称问题。此外，选择哪种特权信息（如解题过程、反馈等）通常具有任务依赖性，难以通过单一视图实现最优效果。

Method: 提出自适应视图自蒸馏（AVSD）方法。该方法通过多视图特权信息，将监督信号拆解为“跨视图共识信号”和“视图特定残差信号”。共识信号提供稳定的更新方向，而残差信号仅在与共识方向一致且强度适中时被有选择性地添加，从而优化训练权重并缓解视图依赖偏差。

Result: 在数学竞赛基准（AIME24、AIME25、HMMT25）上，AVSD 较单视图自蒸馏基线和 GRPO 有显著提升；在 Qwen3-8B 和 Qwen3-4B 模型上，Avg@8 指标分别平均提升了 3.1% 和 2.2%。在代码生成任务（Codeforces、LiveCodeBench v6）上，较单视图基线平均提升了 2.4%。

Conclusion: AVSD 框架通过从多种特权信息视图中提取共识并自适应地融合残差信号，有效解决了传统自蒸馏方法中信息视图依赖及不对称性带来的问题，为语言模型在数学和代码生成任务上的强化学习提供了更稳定、更高效的训练范式。

Abstract: Self-distillation enables language models to learn on-policy from their own trajectories by using the same model as both student and teacher, with the teacher being conditioned on privileged information unavailable to the student. Such information can come in different types or views, such as solutions, demonstrations, feedback, or final answers. This setup provides dense token-level feedback without relying on a separate external model, but creates a fundamental asymmetry: the teacher may rely on view-specific information that the student cannot access at inference time. Moreover, the best type of privileged information is often task-dependent, making it difficult to choose a single teacher view. In this work, we address both these challenges jointly by introducing AVSD (Adaptive-View Self-Distillation), a novel method of self-distillation with multiple privileged-information views, which reconstructs token-level supervision by separating stable cross-view consensus from view-specific residual signals. AVSD identifies the consensus signal shared across views, which provides a reliable update direction, and then selectively adds the view-specific residual signal to adjust the update magnitude when it both aligns with the consensus direction and remains proportionate to the consensus signal. Experiments on math competition benchmarks (AIME24, AIME25, and HMMT25) show that AVSD consistently outperforms both single-view self-distillation baselines and GRPO, achieving average Avg@8 gains of 3.1% and 2.2% over the strongest baselines on Qwen3-8B and Qwen3-4B, respectively. Moreover, on code-generation benchmarks (Codeforces, LiveCodeBench v6) using Qwen3-8B, AVSD outperforms the single-view self-distillation baseline by 2.4% on average.

</details>


### [120] [Design for Manufacturing: A Manufacturability Knowledge-Integrated Reinforcement Learning Framework for Free-Form Pipe Routing in Aeroengines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20644)
*Caicheng Wang,Zili Wang,Shuyou Zhang,Yongzhe Xiang,Zheyi Li,Liangyou Li,Jianrong Tan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为FPRO的强化学习框架，通过将制造工艺限制集成到基于Frenet标架的管路路径优化中，实现了航空发动机管路从设计到六轴自由弯曲制造的一体化流程，大幅提升了设计效率与成品质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 航空发动机复杂管路设计与下游制造环节脱节，导致设计迭代频繁且耗时，亟需一种能够将制造可行性知识整合进设计流程的自动化方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于Frenet标架的管路路由优化（FPRO）框架。利用立方Hermite插值通过曲率和扭率剖面表示管路路径，将制造工艺约束嵌入设计环节，并采用近端策略优化（PPO）算法结合阶段引导的奖励机制进行路径寻优；同时通过统一映射公式将优化路径转化为弯管机的加工运动轨迹。

Result: 实验表明，FPRO生成的路径在平滑度、避障能力、终端对齐精度及制造可行性方面均优于传统的笛卡尔坐标系方法及现有的强化学习基准模型。真实物理验证显示，加工成品与数字化设计高度一致，验证了该方法的工程可行性。

Conclusion: FPRO框架成功实现了航空发动机复杂管路设计与制造的无缝集成，证明了将制造工艺约束直接嵌入强化学习路径规划的有效性，为航空航天领域的高效制造提供了工程化解决方案。

Abstract: Design for manufacturing plays a critical role in advanced aeroengine development, where complex components necessitate careful consideration of manufacturability. However, current practices in pipe routing remain largely decoupled from down-stream manufacturing, leading to labor-intensive, trial-and-error iterations to achieve manufacturable designs. To address this problem, this study proposes the Frenet-based pipe routing optimization (FPRO) framework, a manufacturability knowledge-integrated reinforcement learning approach for free-form pipe design in aeroengines. FPRO formulates the routing problem as a boundary value problem in the Frenet frame. In this framework, the pipe path is represented by curvature and torsion profiles, which are generated using cubic Hermite interpolation. To integrate design and manufacturing, domain-specific manufacturing knowledge is embedded as constraints on the permissible ranges of curvature and torsion. The path optimization is performed using the proximal policy optimization algorithm with stochastic exploration and a stage-guided reward mechanism. A unified mapping formulation then translates the optimized path into motion trajectories for the bending die, enabling direct fabrication on a six-axis free-bending machine. Experimental results demonstrate that FPRO consistently generates collision-free, manufacturable paths with smoother geometric profiles compared to Cartesian-based methods. It also achieves faster convergence and superior performance in terminal alignment, path length, obstacle avoidance, and manufacturability compared to state-of-the-art reinforcement learning baselines. Real-world validation confirms the close geometric correspondence between the manufactured pipe and its digital design, validating the practical feasibility of FPRO.

### [121] [LT2: Linear-Time Looped Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20670)
*Chunyuan Deng,Yizhe Zhang,Rui-Jie Zhu,Yuanyuan Xu,Jiarui Liu,T. S. Eugene Ng,Hanjie Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了LT2（线性时间循环Transformer）架构，通过将二次复杂度的注意力机制替换为高效的线性时间注意力，并结合迭代循环机制，成功在提升计算效率的同时显著增强了语言模型的性能与可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的循环Transformer（Looped Transformers）虽然架构强大，但依赖全注意力机制导致计算复杂度为二次方，限制了其在大规模任务中的扩展速度与计算效率。作者旨在通过引入线性时间注意力机制，解决循环Transformer的高计算成本问题，同时提升其性能表现。

Method: 提出LT2（线性时间循环Transformer）架构系列，用次二次（线性）时间注意机制替代传统的全注意力机制。具体包括：1. LT2-linear（线性注意力）实现迭代记忆细化；2. LT2-sparse（稀疏注意力）实现感受野的渐进扩展；3. LT2-hybrid（混合注意力）通过交替使用线性、稀疏或少量全注意力层，在效率与性能间取得最佳平衡。此外，提出了一种将预训练循环Transformer转换为LT2-hybrid的方法。

Result: LT2架构在受控回忆、状态跟踪及语言建模任务中表现优异。其中，LT2-hybrid（GDN+DSA）以完全线性的计算成本达到了标准循环Transformer的质量；LT2-hybrid（Full+GDN）在性能和效率上均超越了标准循环Transformer。基于此架构的Ouro-hybrid-1.4B模型在10亿token训练量下，性能超越了同规模工业级模型，并具备与40亿参数模型竞争的能力。

Conclusion: 研究表明，循环Transformer结合线性时间注意力机制（LT2）不仅能显著降低计算复杂度，还能通过迭代优化提升模型性能。LT2架构为构建高效、高能力的轻量化语言模型开辟了新路径，证明了在保持计算效率的同时超越传统模型的可行性。

Abstract: Looped Transformers (LT) have emerged as a powerful architecture by iterating their layers multiple times before decoding the final token. However, pairing them with full attention retains quadratic complexity, making them computationally expensive and slow. We introduce LT2 (Linear-Time Looped Transformers), a family of looped architectures that replace quadratic softmax attention with subquadratic, linear-time attention. We study two variants: LT2-linear with linear attention and LT2-sparse with sparse attention. We find that looping uniquely synergizes with these variants: it enables iterative memory refinement in linear attention and progressively expands the effective receptive field in sparse attention. We formalize these benefits theoretically and demonstrate consistent empirical gains across controlled recall, state-tracking, and language modeling tasks. We then explore LT2-hybrid, which combines different attention variants in a looped setting. Two variants are especially promising: LT2-hybrid (GDN+DSA), which interleaves linear and sparse attention to maximize efficiency and matches the standard looped transformer's quality at fully linear-time cost; and LT2-hybrid (Full+GDN), which interleaves GDN with a small fraction of full attention layers to maximize quality, surpassing the standard looped transformer in both performance and efficiency. We also show how to convert a pre-trained LT into an LT2-hybrid model. With about 1B tokens of training, our converted model, Ouro-hybrid-1.4B, outperforms industry-level 1B models and is competitive with industry-level 4B models while retaining the speed benefits of linear-time attention. Together, these results show a clear path toward making looped transformers more scalable and advancing efficient, capable small language models.

### [122] [Modular Multimodal Classification Without Fine-Tuning: A Simple Compositional Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20674)

TL;DR: CoMET 是一种无需训练的多模态分类方法，通过组合冻结的模态编码器、PCA 压缩和表格基础模型，实现了高性能与高可扩展性，证明了模型组合方案的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
