Conclusion: 本文通过建立传输映射的正则性理论，从理论上证明了单步生成模型在拟合PDE诱导分布时的有效性与稳定性，弥补了该领域统计精度理论的不足。

Abstract: Despite the remarkable empirical success of generative models, the available theory on their statistical accuracy in scientific computing remains largely pessimistic. This paper develops a theoretical framework for understanding the regularity of transport maps and the generalization properties of one-step Wasserstein-guided generative models for PDE-induced probability measures. We consider normalized target densities associated with linear elliptic and parabolic equations on bounded domains, as well as diffusion and Fokker--Planck equations on the torus. Under standard structural assumptions, we prove that these target measures satisfy doubling conditions. By combining this fact with regularity theory for optimal transport between doubling measures, we show that the optimal transport map from a uniform source measure to the target measure is Hölder continuous. This regularity yields an approximation-theoretic justification for one-step generative models that learn PDE-induced distributions via a single pushforward map. As a representative instance, we study DeepParticle and derive excess-risk bounds characterizing the discrepancy between the learned map and the population-optimal map. We also establish a robustness estimate under target shift and illustrate the theory with experiments which support the derived rates.

Our customizable execution-aware reward formula captures and optimizes syntax, functional correctness, code style, security, and simulator executability. Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: torchtune 是一个 PyTorch 原生的轻量级 LLM 微调库，它优先考虑代码的模块化和透明度，旨在解决现有框架在灵活性与高性能之间难以平衡的问题，为科研人员提供一个高效的研究工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型微调框架往往在易用性、特定功能和硬件效率之间做妥协，导致框架缺乏灵活性与透明度，难以满足科研人员对深度定制和快速迭代的需求。

Method: 该库采用 PyTorch 原生设计，强调模块化架构，直接调用 PyTorch 基础组件，通过统一的模型构建器、训练配方（Recipes）和分布式训练栈，实现了高度的透明度与可编程性（Hackability）。

Result: 通过与 Axolotl 和 Unsloth 等主流框架的对比实验证明，torchtune 在保证极高灵活性的同时，实现了卓越的训练性能与内存效率，能够胜任多样化的事后训练场景。

Conclusion: torchtune 通过兼顾模块化、可扩展性和高性能，在保持 PyTorch 原生性的同时，为大语言模型的事后训练（Post-training）提供了一个高效、可复现的研发基石。

Abstract: Modern LLMs typically require multistage training pipelines to achieve strong downstream performance, with post-training serving as the main interface for adapting open-weight models. We introduce torchtune, a PyTorch-native library designed to streamline the post-training lifecycle of LLMs, enabling efficient fine-tuning, experimentation, and deployment-oriented workflows. Unlike many existing fine-tuning frameworks, which often optimize for ease of use, specialized recipes, or hardware efficiency at the cost of transparency and extensibility, torchtune emphasizes modularity, hackability, and direct access to the underlying PyTorch components. In this paper, we present the design principles behind torchtune, describe how they are reflected in its model builders, training recipes, and distributed training stack, and evaluate the library across representative post-training settings. We compare against popular fine-tuning frameworks, including Axolotl and Unsloth, and show that torchtune provides strong performance and memory efficiency across many settings while remaining flexible enough for rapid research iteration. These results position torchtune as a practical foundation for reproducible LLMs post-training research.

### [169] [Divide and Contrast: Learning Robust Temporal Features without Augmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21241)
*Abdul-Kazeem Shamba,Kerstin Bach,Gavin Taylor*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Di-COT 是一种新型高效的时间序列自监督学习框架，通过将序列窗口划分为子块并进行对比学习，在无需数据增强的情况下，实现了卓越的表征学习效果和显著提升的计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的时间序列自监督学习方法往往面临高昂的计算成本，或者依赖于在处理复杂时间动态时可能失效的假设。为了减少对标签数据的依赖并同时提升下游任务的性能与计算效率，作者寻求一种更轻量、更鲁棒的表示学习方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Divide and Contrast (Di-COT)”的无监督学习框架。该方法避免了数据增强和多次编码器前向传递，通过将窗口随机划分为少量重叠的子块，并对这些子块进行对比学习，将损失函数计算与序列长度解耦，从而显著提升了训练效率。

Result: 在六个大规模真实数据集以及 UCR 和 UEA 基准测试上的实验结果显示，Di-COT 在分类、聚类、kNN 和跨数据集迁移任务中均达到了最先进（SOTA）的水平，并大幅降低了模型训练所需的时间。

Conclusion: Di-COT 是一种高效且强大的时间序列自监督学习框架，通过子结构对比而非传统的数据增强或逐时间步对比，实现了性能与计算效率的平衡，为处理复杂时间序列数据提供了一种具有竞争力的新范式。

Abstract: Self-supervised learning for time-series representation aims to reduce reliance on labeled data while maintaining strong downstream performance, yet many existing approaches incur high computational costs or rely on assumptions that do not hold across diverse temporal dynamics. In this work, we introduce Divide and Contrast (Di-COT), an unsupervised framework that avoids data augmentation and multiple encoder passes by contrasting informative substructures within a window rather than individual timesteps. Di-COT stochastically partitions each window into a small number of overlapping sub-blocks per iteration, enabling efficient and meaningful contrast while mitigating false positives during temporal transitions. To further improve scalability, we adopt a contrastive objective whose computation depends on the batch size and the number of sub-blocks, making loss computation independent of sequence length. Extensive experiments on six large-scale real-world datasets, as well as the UCR and UEA benchmarks, demonstrate that Di-COT learns semantically structured and transferable representations, achieving state-of-the-art performance on classification, clustering, $k$NN, and cross-dataset transfer, while substantially reducing training time. The source code is publicly available at https://github.com/sfi-norwai/Di-COT.

### [170] [Quantifying Hyperparameter Transfer and the Importance of Embedding Layer Learning Rate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21486)
*Dayal Singh Kalra,Maissam Barkeshli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究量化了超参数迁移效果，揭示了 $μ$P 优于 SP 的核心原因在于嵌入层学习率的设置，并提出通过简单调整嵌入层学习率即可提升传统参数化方法的迁移性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超参数迁移对于大规模语言模型（LLM）的训练至关重要，但现有的关于为何某些参数化方法（如 $μ$P）在超参数迁移上表现优异的理论解释尚不充分，缺乏系统性的量化评估框架。

Method: 1. 建立了一套包含三个核心指标的评估框架，用于量化超参数迁移效果（包括缩放定律拟合质量、外推误差鲁棒性、参数化带来的渐近损失惩罚）；2. 针对 $μ$P 与标准参数化（SP）进行了广泛的消融实验，深入分析两者在 AdamW 优化器下的表现差异。

Result: 1. 发现 $μ$P 相较于 SP 的主要优势在于优化了嵌入层的学习率，解决了 SP 中嵌入层成为训练瓶颈的问题；2. 验证了通过将 SP 的嵌入层学习率增加宽度倍数，可以显著改善训练稳定性和超参数迁移效果；3. 发现权重衰减能改善缩放定律的拟合质量，但在固定每参数 Token 数的设置下，会损害外推过程的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 研究指出，Maximal Update ($μ$P) 在学习率迁移上的优越性主要归功于其对嵌入层学习率的提升，而非复杂的理论机制。通过调整标准参数化（SP）中的嵌入层学习率，可以获得与 $μ$P 相当的效果。此外，权重衰减在优化模型性能方面具有双重作用，需根据训练设置谨慎使用。

Abstract: Hyperparameter transfer allows extrapolating optimal optimization hyperparameters from small to large scales, making it critical for training large language models (LLMs). This is done either by fitting a scaling law to the hyperparameters or by a judicious choice of parameterization, such as Maximal Update ($μ$P), that renders optimal hyperparameters approximately scale invariant. In this paper, we first develop a framework to quantify hyperparameter transfer through three metrics: (1) the quality of the scaling law fit, (2) the robustness to extrapolation errors, and (3) the asymptotic loss penalty due to choice of parameterization. Next, we investigate through a comprehensive series of ablations why $μ$P appears to offer high-quality learning rate transfer relative to standard parameterization (SP), as existing theory is inadequate. We find that the overwhelming benefit of $μ$P relative to SP when training with AdamW arises simply from maximizing the learning rate of the embedding layer. In SP, the embedding layer learning rate acts as a bottleneck that induces training instabilities; increasing it by a factor of width to match $μ$P dramatically smooths out training while improving hyperparameter transfer. We also find that weight decay improves the scaling law fits, while, in the fixed token-per-parameter setting, it hurts the robustness of the extrapolation.

### [171] [Variance Reduction for Expectations with Diffusion Teachers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21489)
*Jesse Bettencourt,Xindi Wu,Matan Atzmon,James Lucas,Jonathan Lorraine*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的文本生成 3D、单步蒸馏及数据归因等下游任务严重依赖冻结的预训练扩散模型，而获取这些模型的梯度需要进行昂贵的蒙特卡洛采样。高昂的计算成本与估计器的高方差成为限制这些流水线效率的主要瓶颈。

Method: 提出了一种计算感知且考虑方差的层次化蒙特卡洛估计框架（CARV）。该方法通过将昂贵的上游计算（如渲染、编码）与廉价的扩散噪声重采样解耦，并结合时间步重要性采样（IS）与分层逆累积分布函数（stratified-inverse-CDF）构造，显著降低了梯度估计的方差和计算成本。

Result: 在文本生成 3D 和数据归因任务中，CARV 实现了 2-3 倍的有效计算加速（大部分源于计算摊销，约 25% 源于 IS+分层采样）。在单步蒸馏中，该方法将梯度方差降低了一个数量级，证明了其降低方差的有效性。

Conclusion: CARV 框架通过分层蒙特卡洛估计和计算感知优化，有效降低了扩散模型梯度估计的方差并提升了计算效率。研究指出，在某些任务（如单步蒸馏）中，梯度方差已不再是主要的性能瓶颈，明确了该方法的适用边界。

Abstract: Pretrained diffusion models serve as frozen teachers feeding downstream pipelines such as text-to-3D, single-step distillation, and data attribution. The teacher gradients these pipelines consume are Monte Carlo (MC) expectations over noise levels and Gaussian noise samples; their estimator variance dominates compute cost because each draw requires expensive upstream work (rendering, simulation, encoding). We introduce CARV, a compute-aware variance-accounting framework that motivates a hierarchical MC estimator: amortize the expensive upstream computation over cheap diffusion-noise resamples, sharpened by timestep importance sampling and a stratified-inverse-CDF construction. In our text-to-3D distillation and attribution experiments, CARV delivers 2-3x effective compute multipliers (most from amortized reuse; ~25% additional from IS+stratification) without changing the objective; in single-step distillation, the same techniques cut gradient variance by an order of magnitude but do not improve downstream FID, marking the regime where MC variance is no longer the bottleneck.

### [172] [On the Cost and Benefit of Chain of Thought: A Learning-Theoretic Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21260)
*Yue Zhang,Zhiyi Dong,Tommaso Cesari,Yongyi Mao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一套思维链（CoT）的学习理论框架，量化了推理过程中中间步骤带来的收益与误差累积带来的代价，并指出稳定性是决定CoT表现优劣的核心因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管思维链（CoT）在大型语言模型中表现出色，但其背后的理论机制尚不明确。现有研究缺乏对CoT如何通过中间推理步骤降低或放大错误，以及何时CoT会产生负面影响的系统性量化理解。

Method: 作者构建了一个学习理论框架，将CoT建模为答案映射与自回归生成中间问题的“链式规则”之间的交互。通过对推理风险进行规范分解，引入了OTR（捕捉CoT带来的收益）和TMR（捕捉误差累积带来的代价），并利用该框架分析了在不同稳定性条件下的误差增长机制（有界、线性及指数增长）。

Result: 1. 证明了推理风险可以分解为OTR和TMR两个分量。2. 揭示了在缺乏结构性稳定性时，TMR可能趋于无限，导致即使单步损失很小，整体推理也会失效。3. 确立了在稳定性条件下的TMR紧凑上界，明确了误差从有界到指数增长的临界条件。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，思维链（CoT）的有效性取决于“预言轨迹风险”（OTR）与“轨迹失配风险”（TMR）之间的权衡。CoT的成功依赖于推理过程的稳定性，若缺乏这种稳定性，即使单步预测准确，长链路推理中的误差累积也可能导致模型性能崩溃。

Abstract: We develop a learning-theoretic framework for understanding Chain of Thought (CoT). We model CoT as the interaction between an answer map and a chain rule that generates intermediate questions autoregressively, and define the reasoning risk of a hypothesis under this interaction. Our first result is a tight canonical decomposition of this risk into two terms with opposing roles: an oracle-trajectory risk (OTR), which captures the benefit of CoT and reduces to a target-domain risk in a domain adaptation problem, and a trajectory-mismatch risk (TMR), which captures the cost of CoT through error accumulation along mismatched reasoning trajectories. We then show that this cost is unavoidable without structure: if any one of the loss, the hypothesis answer map, or the chain rule lacks stability, the TMR can be arbitrarily large even when the OTR is zero and the hypothesis is uniformly close to the ground truth. Conversely, under stability, we prove a tight upper bound on the TMR governed by an exact amplification factor that identifies bounded, linear, and exponential error-growth regimes. Together, these results give a precise theory of when CoT helps, when it hurts, and what controls the transition between the two.

Abstract: Firms increasingly rely on dynamic pricing to respond to evolving customer demand, yet in many applications they observe only the revenue generated by a single posted price in each period. At the same time, market conditions may shift gradually or abruptly due to changes in customer preferences, competition, or external shocks. These features create two intertwined challenges: learning the revenue--demand relationship from limited feedback and adapting pricing decisions to a changing environment. We study how a seller can learn and earn effectively under these constraints, without assuming a specific parametric form for demand. We develop a learning framework that updates prices using revenue-based gradient approximations constructed from one observation per period. To address environmental changes, we incorporate a restarting mechanism that periodically refreshes the learning process so that outdated information is discounted. When the degree of nonstationarity is unknown, we further introduce a meta-learning layer to adaptively hedge across multiple restarting schedules. ### [174] [A Mechanistic Study of Tabular Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21288)
*Marin Biloš,James T. Wilson,Anderson Schneider,Yuriy Nevmyvaka*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管表格基础模型在分类与回归任务中表现出相似的精度，但目前尚不清楚它们是否在执行相同的上下文算法、排列不变性的来源为何，以及针对其内部机制的鲁棒性如何。因此，需要从机理层面深入探讨这些模型的工作原理。

Method: 研究采用了因果干预分析（causal intervention）、表示层分析、排列不变性测试，以及针对特定推断机制设计的对抗性扰动（包括hub和rank攻击）来解析模型行为。

Result: 1. 模型实现了本质上不同的基于相似性的读出机制；2. 所谓“表示崩溃”在实际应用中并非严重问题；3. 排列不变性直接归因于特定的位置参数；4. 通过针对性设计的扰动，成功重现了模型预期的失效模式。

Conclusion: 本文通过因果干预分析，揭示了表格基础模型并非表现得“千篇一律”，而是采用了基于不同相似度度量的机制（如加权投票或类条件均值）。这些模型的排列不变性源于特定的位置参数，且其鲁棒性存在针对性的机制脆弱性。研究明确了决定这些模型精度与失效模式的归纳偏置。

Abstract: Tabular foundation models with different architectures converge in accuracy across a range of classification and regression tasks. This raises questions a leaderboard cannot answer: (i) whether the models execute the same in-context algorithm, (ii) where row, column, and class-permutation invariances originate, and (iii) how robust they are under perturbations engineered against the inferred mechanism. We characterize all three. The model families realize qualitatively distinct similarity-based readouts: from an attention-weighted vote over context labels to a class-conditional mean readout, each confirmed by causal intervention. We find that the representation collapse highlighted in prior work is not a practical concern for them. Each model's permutation invariances trace to specific positional parameters whose removal preserves accuracy and makes approximate invariance exact. Perturbations engineered against each readout reproduce predicted failure modes; hub and rank attacks isolate them from refit baselines. Together these results give a mechanistic account of contemporary tabular foundation models and identify which inductive biases govern both their accuracy and characteristic failures.

### [175] [Automatic Discovery of Disease Subgroups by Contrasting with Healthy Controls](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21301)

Method: Deep UCSL 采用深度特征提取器学习判别性表示空间；设计了一种基于潜在聚类与标签条件联合似然的新颖损失函数；利用期望最大化（EM）策略在亚组推理和特征编码器更新之间交替优化；并引入正则化项强制模型过滤掉患者与健康对照组共享的变异，仅捕捉病理特异性信息。

Abstract: In biomedical Subgroup Discovery, practitioners are interested in discovering interpretable and homogeneous subgroups within a group of patients. In this paper, assuming that healthy subjects (i.e., controls) share common but irrelevant factors of variation with the patients, we motivate and develop a Contrastive Subgroup Discovery method, entitled Deep UCSL. By contrasting patients with controls, Deep UCSL identifies subgroups driven solely by pathological factors, ignoring common variability shared with healthy subjects. Our framework employs a deep feature extractor to learn a discriminative representation space. Mathematically, we derive a novel loss based on the conditional joint likelihood of latent clusters and patient/control labels, optimized via an Expectation-Maximization strategy alternating between subgroup inference and feature encoder updates. A regularization term further encourages representations to capture disease-specific variability while ignoring variability shared with controls. Compared to previous related works, our approach quantitatively improves the quality of the estimated subgroups, as demonstrated on a MNIST example and four distinct real medical imaging datasets. Code and datasets are available at: https://github.com/rlouiset/deep_ucsl.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在联邦学习中，由于客户端数据分布异构，简单的加权平均聚合会导致全局更新与某些特定客户端的本地更新目标冲突，从而引发模型在这些客户端上的性能下降（即“客户端漂移”或性能恶化）。现有方法难以高效且准确地调和这些冲突。

Method: CRAFT将聚合过程建模为几何修正问题，旨在寻找一个既接近参考方向又满足“无冲突对齐”约束的更新向量。该方法推导出了该约束优化问题的闭式解（Closed-form expression），避免了迭代求解带来的计算负担，并引入了逐层适应（Layer-wise adaptation）机制以处理不同特征粒度下的冲突。

Result: 在多个异构基准测试上的实验表明，CRAFT在提升全局模型整体准确率的同时，降低了客户端之间的性能差异（即提升了公平性），优于现有的先进基准算法。此外，其闭式解设计保证了计算的高效性。

Conclusion: CRAFT通过几何约束视角有效解决了联邦学习中异构数据导致的客户端更新冲突问题，在提升全局模型精度的同时，显著改善了各客户端之间的性能公平性。

Abstract: The aggregation of conflicting client updates remains a fundamental bottleneck in federated learning (FL) under heterogeneous data distributions. Naive averaging can produce a global update that improves the global objective while conflicting with specific clients, causing degradation for those clients. In this work, we propose CRAFT (Conflict-Resolved Aggregation for Federated Training), a new aggregation framework that treats the global update as a geometric correction problem. We formulate aggregation as finding the update closest to a reference direction while satisfying conflict-free alignment constraints. We derive a closed-form expression for the constrained optimization problem, avoiding the computational overhead of iterative solvers. Furthermore, we use a layer-wise adaptation to address conflicts at varying feature granularities. We provide a theoretical analysis showing that CRAFT promotes a common-descent structure and mitigates conflicts through its projection geometry. Extensive experiments on heterogeneous benchmarks demonstrate that CRAFT improves the accuracy of the global model while reducing performance disparity across clients compared with state-of-the-art baselines. The source code for CRAFT is available at https://github.com/tum-pbs/CRAFT.

</details>


### [177] [Optimized Federated Knowledge Distillation with Distributed Neural Architecture Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21322)

TL;DR: FedKDNAS 是一种新型联邦学习框架，通过在客户端进行神经架构搜索并结合服务器协调的知识蒸馏，有效解决了联邦学习中数据异构、系统差异及高昂通信成本的难题，实现了资源受限场景下的高精度与高效率兼顾。

Motivation: 现有的联邦学习方法多假设客户端采用固定架构，这限制了模型在处理复杂且异构的数据分布（non-IID）时的适应性，也难以满足边缘设备在性能和资源开销之间的差异化约束。现有方法在处理系统异构性和通信效率平衡方面存在局限，无法在真实场景下实现最优的权衡。

Method: 提出了 FedKDNAS 框架，核心机制包括：1. 客户端侧神经架构搜索，使设备能根据自身计算资源和数据复杂度选择合适的轻量化模型；2. 混合训练目标，结合监督学习与基于公共参考集的知识蒸馏；3. 服务器端协调机制，通过聚合和平滑各客户端的预测输出（Logits）生成稳定的全局蒸馏目标，实现跨异构模型的知识迁移。

Result: 在六个基准数据集上的对比实验显示，FedKDNAS 在非独立同分布（non-IID）条件下精度提升达 15%，客户端 CPU 使用率降低约 28%，通信开销最高减少了 44 倍，在多种主流联邦学习基准算法中展现出卓越的帕累托效率。

Conclusion: FedKDNAS 证明了结合神经架构搜索（NAS）与知识蒸馏（KD）是解决异构联邦学习挑战的有效方案，能够在极具挑战的非独立同分布（non-IID）场景下，实现模型精度、计算效率与通信开销之间的最优帕累托平衡，为资源受限的边缘设备提供了灵活且高效的部署范式。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) enables collaborative model training without centralizing data. However, real-world deployments must simultaneously address statistical heterogeneity across client data (non-IID), system heterogeneity in device capabilities, and communication efficiency. Existing FL approaches mitigate these challenges through improved aggregation, personalization, or knowledge distillation, but they almost universally assume a fixed client architecture, limiting adaptability to heterogeneous data complexity and hardware constraints. This architectural constraint often leads to suboptimal trade-offs between accuracy and efficiency in real-world FL systems. This work introduces FedKDNAS, a distillation-driven FL framework that combines client-side neural architecture selection with distillation of server-coordinated knowledge. Each client autonomously selects a lightweight model under accuracy-resource constraints. It then trains it locally using a hybrid objective combining supervised learning and knowledge distillation and shares only predictions on a public reference set. The server then aggregates and smooths these predictions, optionally combining them with a teacher model, to produce stable distillation targets for the next round. Extensive evaluation on six datasets against six representative FL baselines (FedAvg, Ditto, FedMD, FedDF, FedDistill, Local-KD) demonstrates that FedKDNAS consistently achieves superior Pareto efficiency, improving accuracy by up to 15\% under non-IID conditions, reducing client CPU usage by approximately 28\%, and decreasing communication overhead by up to 44 times while maintaining lightweight logit-based communication.

This work provides a systematic analysis of both direct and iterative triangular inversion algorithms, targeting methods that are rich in matrix products, and, therefore, have the potential to efficiently utilize modern hardware. To that end, our analysis covers a broad spectrum of mathematical and practical aspects, with a heavy focus on numerical stability, computational complexity, and, ultimately, hardware efficiency and practical considerations. In the proposed method, time domain PD pulses are characterized using pulse amplitude, width, and area, and mapped into a visual pattern where amplitude and area define the coordinate axes and width is encoded by color. The generated AWA patterns are used to distinguish six single and mixed PD source conditions: corona, internal, surface, corona+internal, corona+surface, and internal+surface. ### [180] [Adaptive Signal Resuscitation: Channel-wise Post-Pruning Repair for Sparse Vision Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21426)
*Qishi Zhan,Ziheng Chen,Minxuan Hu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对一键剪枝在高稀疏度下的精度崩溃问题，本文提出了“自适应信号复苏”（ASR）方法。它通过通道级的信号方差匹配和收缩规则，在无需重新训练的情况下，有效修复剪枝造成的通道受损，显著提升了模型的剪枝后性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一键式幅度剪枝在极高稀疏度下会导致严重的精度下降。作者认为这是由于现有修复方法采用层级粒度，无法处理同一层内受损程度不一的通道，导致过度放大受损通道的信号而产生错误。

Method: 提出了一种无需训练的通道级修复方法——自适应信号复苏（ASR）。该方法针对每个输出通道估计方差匹配修正值，并引入数据驱动的收缩规则来抑制不可靠的通道修正，在批归一化（BatchNorm）重校准前进行处理，仅需少量校准集的前向传播即可完成。

Result: 在多个数据集、卷积架构以及非结构化和结构化稀疏设置下，ASR 均优于现有的层级修复方法。在 ResNet-50 的 90% 稀疏度下，ASR 将 CIFAR-10 的 Top-1 精度恢复至 55.6%，显著高于层级修复（41.0%）和仅使用 BatchNorm 重校准（28.0%）的效果。

Conclusion: 本文提出的自适应信号复苏（ASR）方法通过精细化的通道级修复，有效解决了高稀疏度下一键剪枝导致的精度崩溃问题。研究证明，修复粒度与受损粒度的匹配对于模型剪枝后的恢复至关重要，且数据驱动的收缩规则能显著增强修复的稳定性。

Abstract: One-shot magnitude pruning can cause severe accuracy collapse in the high-sparsity regime, even when the pruning mask preserves the largest weights. We argue that this failure reflects a granularity mismatch in post-pruning repair. Under global magnitude pruning, nearly collapsed channels can coexist with channels that retain informative activation variance within the same layer. Existing layer-wise activation repair methods apply a single correction to the whole layer, and can therefore over-amplify damaged channels while trying to restore the layer-level signal. We propose Adaptive Signal Resuscitation (ASR), a training-free channel-wise repair method that matches the granularity of repair to the granularity of damage. ASR estimates a variance-matching correction for each output channel and stabilizes it with a data-driven shrinkage rule, suppressing unreliable corrections for channels with weak post-pruning signal while preserving corrections for healthier channels. Applied before BatchNorm recalibration, ASR requires only forward passes on a small calibration set and no retraining. Across three datasets, four convolutional architectures, and both unstructured and structured sparsity settings, ASR generally improves over layer-wise repair, with the clearest gains in high-sparsity regimes. On ResNet-50 at 90% sparsity, ASR recovers 55.6% top-1 accuracy on CIFAR-10, compared with 41.0% for layer-wise repair and 28.0% for BatchNorm-only recalibration. Ablations show that naive channel-wise variance matching is insufficient, and that shrinkage stabilizes post-pruning repair.

### [181] [Polynomial-Time Robust Multiclass Linear Classification under Gaussian Marginals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21428)
*Ilias Diakonikolas,Giannis Iakovidis,Mingchen Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对高斯分布下的多类线性分类器不可知学习问题，克服了传统多类感知机的局限性，提出了首个在多项式时间内实现维度无关误差保证的稳健学习框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在不可知学习场景下，多类线性分类器（$k \ge 3$）的算法理论远不如二分类（$k=2$）成熟，现有的稳健算法在精度上存在指数级复杂度和表示规模的依赖，缺乏针对多分类的高效、维度无关的误差保证算法。

Method: 本文提出了基于“成对不当学习”（pairwise improper learning）的框架来处理通用类别数 $k$ 的分类问题，并开发了基于“定位”（localization-based）的优化技术，旨在提高对几何正则类别的学习精度，同时揭示了标准多类感知机算法在样本复杂度和更新次数上存在的超多项式障碍。

Result: 1. 证明了标准多类感知机在处理高斯边缘分布时存在超多项式复杂度的基本障碍；2. 针对一般 $k$ 类问题，实现了误差为 $\widetilde O(k^{3/2}\sqrt{\mathrm{opt}})+ε$ 的高效学习器；3. 针对 $k=3$ 的情况实现了 $O(\mathrm{opt})+ε$ 的最优误差，对于几何正则分类器实现了 $\mathrm{poly}(k)\mathrm{opt}+ε$ 的误差保证。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过成对不当学习（pairwise improper learning）和基于定位的框架，可以实现多类线性分类器的高效不可知学习，克服了传统感知机算法在多分类问题上的局限性，并实现了与类别数相关的多项式时间复杂度。

Abstract: We study the task of agnostic learning of multiclass linear classifiers under the Gaussian distribution. Given labeled examples $(x, y)$ from a distribution over $\mathbb{R}^d \times [k]$, with Gaussian $x$-marginal, the goal is to output a hypothesis whose error is comparable to that of the best $k$-class linear classifier. While the binary case $k=2$ has a well-developed algorithmic theory, much less is known for $k \ge 3$. Even for $k=3$, prior robust algorithms incur exponential dependence on the inverse of the desired accuracy in both complexity and representation size. In this work, we develop new structural results for multiclass linear classifiers and use them to design fully polynomial-time robust learners with dimension-independent error guarantees. Our first result shows that the standard multiclass perceptron algorithm requires super-polynomially many samples and updates, even with clean labels and Gaussian marginals, revealing a basic obstruction absent in the binary case. Our main positive result is a pairwise improper-learning framework which yields an efficient learner with error $\widetilde O(k^{3/2}\sqrt{\mathrm{opt}})+ε$ for general $k$. Additionally, we develop a sharper localization-based framework which leads to error $O(\mathrm{opt})+ε$ for $k=3$, and error $\mathrm{poly}(k)\mathrm{opt}+ε$ for geometrically regular $k$-class linear classifiers.

</details>

Although multi-constellations GNSS effectively increase the number of available satellites, the inclusion of degraded signals can lead to severe positioning errors. This study proposes a machine learning framework for the weighted least squares (WLS) algorithm incorporating activation functions to enhance positioning accuracy. Several signal quality indicators are employed as training features for ensemble learning algorithms to identify poor quality signals by providing quality scores. Then, activation functions are employed to transform the machine learning predicted scores to appropriate weights for WLS positioning. To evaluate the performance of our approach, experiments are conducted using real-world datasets from Hong Kong and Tokyo urban areas. The proposed algorithm maintains comparable level of performance when trained on data from other regions with similar levels of urbanization.

### [183] [Is Fixing Schema Graphs Necessary? Full-Resolution Graph Structure Learning for Relational Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21475)
*Yi Huang,Qingyun Sun,Jia Li,Xingcheng Fu,Jianxin Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有关系深度学习中图结构固定的缺陷，FROG 提出了一种可联合优化图结构与表示学习的新框架，通过学习表角色分配和施加函数依赖约束，显著提升了关系预测任务的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的关系深度学习（RDL）方法通常依赖于固定不变的图结构来保持关系语义（全分辨率属性）。这种硬编码的结构限制了模型的表达能力和适应性，无法灵活地从数据中学习最优的结构表示。因此，研究者旨在打破这种限制，实现图结构与深度学习模型的联合优化。

Method: 提出了一种名为 FROG 的全分辨率且可优化的图结构学习框架。核心方法包括：1. 将关系结构建模为可学习的“表角色”问题，允许表在消息传递中灵活充当节点或边；2. 设计角色驱动的消息传递机制，实现图结构与 GNN 表示的联合优化；3. 引入函数依赖约束，以确保跨表和实体层面的语义一致性。

Result: 在多项实验中，FROG 框架的表现优于现有的多种关系预测方法。此外，实验结果揭示了不同的“表角色”如何影响下游任务的表现，为后续关系数据库的图构建提供了理论依据和实践指导。

Conclusion: FROG 证明了在关系深度学习中，将图结构视为可优化的实体（而非固定结构）能够显著提升模型性能。通过表角色建模和函数依赖约束，该框架不仅增强了预测精度，还为理解关系数据库中的结构语义提供了新视角。

Abstract: Relational prediction tasks are fundamental in many real-world applications, where data are naturally stored in relational databases (RDBs). Relational Deep Learning (RDL) addresses this problem by modeling RDBs as graphs and applying graph neural networks (GNNs) for end-to-end learning. However, the full-resolution property is commonly adopted as a design principle in graph construction for RDBs to preserve relational semantics, which leads most existing methods to rely on fixed graph structures. In this paper, we propose FROG, a Full-Resolution and Optimizable Graph Structure Learning} framework for RDL that formulates relational structure learning as a learnable table role modeling problem, allowing tables to contribute as nodes and edges in message passing. We further design role-driven message passing mechanisms to capture relational semantics, enabling joint optimization of graph structure and GNN representations. To ensure semantic consistency, we introduce functional dependency constraints that regularize representations across table and entity levels. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method outperforms existing approaches and reveal how table roles impact downstream tasks, offering new insights into graph construction for RDL

</details>


### [184] [Equilibrium Reasoners: Learning Attractors Enables Scalable Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21488)
*Benhao Huang,Zhengyang Geng,Zico Kolter*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了“平衡推理器”（EqR），通过将推理过程形式化为向任务条件吸引子收敛的动力系统，证明了通过增加测试时迭代和轨迹采样，可以使模型在无需外部验证器的情况下，显著提升对复杂推理任务的泛化能力和准确度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管迭代式潜空间模型在推理任务中表现出色，但其超出记忆模式的泛化能力及其内部机制尚不明确。作者旨在验证泛化推理是否源于学习“任务条件吸引子”（即潜动力系统的稳定不动点对应有效解）。

Method: 提出了“平衡推理器”（Equilibrium Reasoners, EqR），通过学习任务条件的吸引子，使潜空间动力系统在测试时通过迭代收敛到有效解。该方法通过增加迭代深度（depth）和聚合多重初始化的随机轨迹（breadth）来实现测试时计算的扩展。

Result: EqR 模型在 Sudoku-Extreme 任务中表现出显著的性能提升，通过将测试时计算扩展至相当于 40,000 层，模型准确率从前馈模型的 2.6% 提升至超过 99%。实验证实测试时扩展的收益与模型向解对齐的吸引子收敛紧密相关，且能够根据任务难度自适应分配计算资源。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，学习到的吸引子（attractor）景观为理解迭代潜空间模型中的可扩展推理提供了一个有效的机制视角，证明了通过测试时计算（test-time compute）的扩展可以显著提升模型在复杂推理任务中的性能。

Abstract: Scaling test-time compute by iteratively updating a latent state has emerged as a powerful paradigm for reasoning. Yet the internal mechanisms that enable these iterative models to generalize beyond memorized patterns remain unclear. We hypothesize that generalizable reasoning arises from learning task-conditioned attractors: latent dynamical systems whose stable fixed points correspond to valid solutions.
  We formalize this process through Equilibrium Reasoners (EqR), which enable test-time scaling without external verifiers or task-specific priors. EqR scales internal dynamics along two axes: depth, by running more iterations, and breadth, by aggregating stochastic trajectories from multiple initializations. Empirically, gains from test-time scaling are tightly coupled with stronger convergence toward solution-aligned attractors.
  This attractor perspective allows neural networks to adaptively allocate test-time compute based on task difficulty. While simple cases converge within 1 to 5 iteration steps, harder cases benefit from massive test-time scaling. By unrolling up to the equivalent of 40,000 layers, scalable latent reasoning boosts accuracy from 2.6% for feedforward models to over 99% on Sudoku-Extreme. These results suggest that learned attractor landscapes provide a useful mechanistic lens for understanding scalable reasoning in iterative latent models.

</details>

### [185] [SOLAR: A Self-Optimizing Open-Ended Autonomous Agent for Lifelong Learning and Continual Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20189)
*Nitin Vetcha,Dianbo Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大模型在动态环境中难以持续适应且易产生灾难性遗忘的问题，论文提出了 SOLAR 框架，通过元学习和强化学习使模型能够自主优化适应策略，在保持知识稳定性的同时实现高效的终身自主学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在动态、非平稳的现实世界中面临挑战，传统的微调（FT）方式在面对数据流时容易出现灾难性遗忘，且计算成本高昂，且难以进行大规模手动数据标注。因此，需要一种能够自主进行终身学习和适应的机制。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SOLAR（自我优化终身自主推理器）的框架：1. 使用参数级元学习将模型权重作为探索环境；2. 采用多级强化学习策略，使智能体能够自主发现并执行针对未见领域的适应策略；3. 维护一个不断演进的有效修改策略知识库，作为情景记忆缓冲区，以解决灾难性遗忘问题。

Result: 实验结果表明，SOLAR 在常识推理、数学、医疗、编码、社交及逻辑推理等多个领域的任务中均优于强基准模型，有效验证了其在演变环境中实现终身适应的性能。

Conclusion: SOLAR 展示了大型语言模型在动态环境中实现终身自主学习的可行性。通过将模型权重视为探索环境并利用元学习与强化学习相结合，该框架有效地平衡了模型的稳定性与可塑性，为构建能够持续进化且无需大规模微调的智能体提供了新的技术范式。

Abstract: Despite the remarkable success of large language models (LLMs), they still face bottlenecks while deploying in dynamic, real-world settings with primary challenges being concept drift and the high cost of gradient-based adaptation. Traditional fine-tuning (FT) struggles to adapt to non-stationary data streams without resulting in catastrophic for getting or requiring extensive manual data curation. To address these limitations within the streaming and continual learning paradigm, we propose the Self-Optimizing Lifelong Autonomous Reasoner (SOLAR) which is an open-ended autonomous agent that leverages parameter-level meta-learning to self-improve, treating model weights as an environment for exploration. It initiates the process by consolidating a strong prior over common-sense knowledge making it effective for transfer-learning. By utilizing a multi-level reinforcement learning approach, SOLAR autonomously discovers adaptation strategies, enabling efficient test-time adaptation to unseen domains. Crucially, SOLAR maintains an evolving knowledge base of valid modification strategies, implicitly acting as an episodic memory buffer to balance plasticity (adaptation to new tasks) and stability (retention of meta-knowledge). Experiments demonstrate that SOLAR outperforms strong baselines on common-sense, mathematical, medical, coding, social and logical reasoning tasks, marking a significant step toward autonomous agents capable of lifelong adaptation in evolving environments.

</details>


### [186] [AgentCo-op: Retrieval-Based Synthesis of Interoperable Multi-Agent Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20425)
*Shuaike Shen,Wenduo Cheng,Shike Wang,Mingqian Ma,Jian Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentCo-op 是一个新型检索式合成框架，通过类型化构件编排和局部修复机制，能够无需全局重构即可利用现有工具与智能体自动构建复杂的开放世界科学工作流，在提升性能的同时降低了成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在开放式科学研究场景中，缺乏标准化的训练集、可靠的评估指标以及工具与智能体之间的标准接口，使得设计多智能体工作流变得极其困难。研究旨在解决如何从现有资源中高效构建可执行且可审计的科学工作流的问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为 AgentCo-op 的检索式合成框架。该方法通过类型化构件（typed artifact）传递来实现技能、工具和智能体的组合，并引入了有界的自引导局部修复（bounded self-guided local repair）机制，在执行出现故障时对相关组件进行修复，无需重新设计或进行全局拓扑搜索。

Result: 在两个基因组学案例研究中成功构建了可审计的工作流；在六个编码、数学和问答基准测试中，AgentCo-op 在其中四个取得最佳表现，并在统一骨干模型下达到最佳平均得分，同时显著降低了单个任务的计算成本。

Conclusion: AgentCo-op 证明了基于检索的合成方法能够有效扩展自动化智能体工作流设计，使其超越了基准测试优化的范畴，实现从现有智能体、工具和构件中构建开放世界的科学工作流，且具有高效率和可审计性。

Abstract: Designing multi-agent workflows is especially difficult in open-ended scientific settings where tasks lack curated training sets, reliable scalar evaluation metrics, and standardized interfaces between existing tools and agents. We propose AgentCo-op, a retrieval-based synthesis framework that composes reusable skills, tools, and external agents into executable workflows through typed artifact handoffs, then applies bounded self-guided local repair to implicated components when execution evidence indicates failure. In two open-world genomics case studies, AgentCo-op composes independently developed scientific agents and external tool repositories into auditable workflows without redesigning them or running global topology search. It coordinates specialized agents for spatial transcriptomics and gene-set interpretation to enable collaborative discovery from spatial transcriptomics data, and builds a parallel workflow for cross-modality marker analysis on single-cell multiome data. AgentCo-op can also import a searched workflow as a structural prior and improve it by grounding nodes with retrieved components and applying local repair, showing that synthesis and search are complementary. On six coding, math, and question-answering benchmarks, AgentCo-op achieves the best result on four benchmarks and the best average score under a unified backbone setting, while consistently reducing per-task cost relative to multi-agent baselines. Together, these results suggest that retrieval-based synthesis can extend automated agentic workflow design beyond benchmark-optimized agent graphs to open-world workflows built from existing agents, tools, and typed artifacts.

</details>


### [187] [\ECUAS{n}: A family of metrics for principled evaluation of uncertainty-augmented systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20490)
*Lautaro Estienne,Erik Ernst,Matías Vera,Pablo Piantanida,Luciana Ferrer*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对现有不确定性增强（UA）系统评估方法不够全面的问题，本文提出了 ECUAS_n 指标体系。通过引入可调参数，该方法能将预测准确性与不确定性质量统一在同一个基于适当评分规则的框架下，为不同决策需求提供更精准的性能评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高风险自动化决策中，评估 UA 系统（输出预测及不确定性分数）的性能至关重要。作者认为目前领域内通用的评估方法（如分离评估、固定拒绝成本或覆盖-风险曲线积分）存在局限性，无法全面反映系统在不同应用需求下的实际决策价值，因此需要一种更具通用性和灵活性的评估框架。

Method: 作者提出了一系列名为 ECUAS_n 的新型评估指标。该方法基于适当评分规则（Proper Scoring Rules）进行建模，通过引入参数 n 来显式调节错误预测成本与不确定性估计不准确之间的权衡，从而量化 UA 系统在不同决策成本下的整体表现。

Result: 通过理论分析和在多个分类与生成数据集（包括 TriviaQA 的标注子集）上的实验验证，证明了 ECUAS_n 指标在评估 UA 系统性能方面的有效性。实验结果显示，该方法相比传统指标更能直观地反映系统在不同应用场景下的决策成本效益。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的 ECUAS 度量标准为评估不确定性增强（UA）系统的整体决策性能提供了一个统一且灵活的框架。与传统方法相比，该指标能够更好地捕捉预测准确性和不确定性质量之间的权衡，从而使系统更适用于具有不同成本敏感性的实际高风险应用场景。

Abstract: In high-stakes automated decision-making, access to predictive uncertainty is essential for enabling users -- human or downstream systems -- to accept or reject predictions based on application-specific cost trade-offs. Such uncertainty-augmented (UA) systems -- i.e., systems that output both predictions and uncertainty scores -- are currently being assessed in the literature in a variety of ways, using separate metrics to evaluate the predictions and the uncertainty scores, setting a cost function with a fixed rejection cost or integrating over a coverage-risk curve. We argue that these evaluation approaches are inadequate for assessing overall performance of the UA system for decision making under uncertainty and propose a novel family of metrics, \ECUAS{n}, formulated as proper scoring rules for the task of interest. The parameter $n$ controls the trade-off between the cost of incorrect predictions and imperfect uncertainties depending on the needs of the use-case. We demonstrate the advantages of the \ECUAS{n} metrics both theoretically and empirically, through experiments on diverse classification and generation datasets, including a manually annotated subset of TriviaQA.

</details>


### [188] [AgentAtlas: Beyond Outcome Leaderboards for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20530)
*Parsa Mazaheri,Kasra Mazaheri*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对现有智能体评估基准碎片化的问题，提出了多维度的 AgentAtlas 评估框架。研究发现，智能体的表现高度依赖提示词中的显式指导，单一的准确率指标已不足以评估现代智能体，必须引入更细致的行为与错误分类法来衡量其综合能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体（Agent）应用场景日益广泛，但现有的评估基准碎片化严重，且单纯依赖“任务成功率”这一单一指标已无法有效评估智能体在代码、操作系统及复杂工具环境下的真实能力与鲁棒性。

Method: 本文构建了一套系统的评估框架 AgentAtlas，包含：(1) 六状态控制决策分类法；(2) 九类别轨迹失败分析法；(3) 区分“标签提示”与“无提示”的对比方法，以剥离模型对提示工程的依赖；(4) 针对现有十五个基准测试的覆盖范围审计与六大行为轴映射分析。

Result: 实验表明，移除提示词中的显式标签菜单会导致所有参与测试的模型（包含闭源与开源模型）轨迹准确率下降 14-40 个百分点，最终收敛至 0.54-0.62 的区间。此外，没有单一模型能在控制准确性、轨迹诊断及工具上下文利用率三个维度上同时获胜。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 AgentAtlas 方法论揭示了单一准确率指标已无法满足评估复杂智能体模型的需求，必须通过多维度的分类框架和行为轴度量来全面衡量智能体的能力。评估结果表明，模型能力高度依赖提示词中的显式指导，且目前尚无单一模型能在所有控制、诊断和效用维度上表现最优。

Abstract: Large language model agents now act on codebases, browsers, operating systems, calendars, files, and tool ecosystems, but the benchmarks used to evaluate them are fragmented: each emphasizes a different unit of measurement (final task success, tool-call validity, repeated-pass consistency, trajectory safety, or attack robustness). A line of 2024-2025 work has converged on the diagnosis that a single accuracy column is no longer the right unit of comparison for deployable agents. AgentAtlas extends this line of work with four components: (i) a six-state control-decision taxonomy (Act / Ask / Refuse / Stop / Confirm / Recover); (ii) a nine-category trajectory-failure taxonomy with two orthogonal hierarchical labels (primary_error_source, impact); (iii) a taxonomy-aware vs. taxonomy-blind methodology that measures how much of a model's apparent capability comes from the supervision in the prompt; and (iv) a benchmark-coverage audit mapping fifteen agent benchmarks against six behavioral axes. To demonstrate the methodology we run a small fixed eight-model set (1,342 generated items, four frontier closed and four open-weight) under both prompt modes. Removing the explicit label menu drops every model's trajectory accuracy by 14-40 pp to a tight 0.54-0.62 floor regardless of family, and no single model wins on all three of control accuracy, trajectory diagnosis, and tool-context utility retention. We treat the synthetic run as a measurement-protocol demonstration, not a benchmark release.

</details>


### [189] [Mahjax: A GPU-Accelerated Mahjong Simulator for Reinforcement Learning in JAX](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20577)
*Soichiro Nishimori,Shinri Okano,Keigo Habara,Sotetsu Koyamada,Eason Yu,Masashi Sugiyama*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Mahjax 是一个基于 JAX 的高性能立直麻将训练环境，通过 GPU 并行化极大地提升了环境交互效率，为研究复杂环境下的强化学习提供了一个强大的开源工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 立直麻将具备多玩家、不完全信息、随机性和高维状态空间等复杂特性，是研究强化学习的理想场景。现有研究多依赖人类棋谱监督学习，缺乏通用的从零开始（tabula rasa）学习框架。为了推动该领域的研究，作者旨在构建一个高效、并行化的麻将训练环境。

Method: 作者开发了 Mahjax，这是一个基于 JAX 框架完全向量化的立直麻将环境。该方法利用 JAX 的即时编译（JIT）和自动微分能力，在 GPU 上实现了大规模的并行 Rollout（模拟），从而大幅加快了环境交互速度。

Result: Mahjax 在八块 NVIDIA A100 GPU 上，对于无红宝牌规则可达到每秒 200 万步的吞吐量，对于有红宝牌规则可达到每秒 100 万步。实验证明，该环境能够有效支持智能体进行强化学习训练，并显著提升其在基准策略下的排名表现。

Conclusion: Mahjax 为立直麻将的强化学习研究提供了一个高效、可扩展的基准环境，证实了基于 JAX 的向量化实现能够极大提升训练效率，并为未来探索从零开始（tabula rasa）的强化学习算法提供了强有力的支持。

Abstract: Riichi Mahjong is a multi-player, imperfect-information game characterized by stochasticity and high-dimensional state spaces. These attributes present a unique combination of challenges that mirror complex real-world decision-making problems in reinforcement learning. While prior research has heavily relied on supervised learning from human play logs to pre-train the policy, algorithms capable of learning \textit{tabula rasa} (from scratch) offer greater potential for general applicability, as evidenced by the AlphaZero lineage. To facilitate such research, we introduce \textbf{Mahjax}, a fully vectorized Riichi Mahjong environment implemented in JAX to enable large-scale rollout parallelization on Graphics Processing Units (GPUs). We also provide a high-quality visualization tool to streamline debugging and interaction with trained agents. Experimental results demonstrate that Mahjax achieves throughputs of up to \textbf{2 million} and \textbf{1 million steps per second} on eight NVIDIA A100 GPUs under the no-red and red rules, respectively. Furthermore, we validate the environment's utility for reinforcement learning by showing that agents can be trained effectively to improve their rank against baseline policies.

</details>


### [190] [COAgents: Multi-Agent Framework to Learn and Navigate Routing Problems Search Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20618)
*Oleksandr Yakovenko,Mahdi Mostajabdaveh,Cheikh Ahmed,Abdullah Ali Sivas,Xiaorui Li,Zirui Zhou,Mao Kun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: COAgents 是一种用于解决车辆路径问题的协作多智能体框架，它通过动态构建搜索图并利用智能体协同控制搜索的强化与探索过程，在多个基准测试中超越了现有先进的神经求解器和传统算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 车辆路径问题（VRP）具有高度的组合复杂性，在大规模场景下计算困难。传统的启发式算法依赖人工设计的规则，难以在不同场景中泛化；而端到端深度学习方法往往难以处理复杂的约束条件，且缺乏针对不同搜索阶段（强化 vs 探索）的精准控制。

Method: 提出了一种名为 COAgents 的协作多智能体框架，将搜索过程视为图的演化：通过动态构建“部分搜索图”（PSG），训练节点选择、动作选择和跳跃（Jump）三个协同工作的智能体。该方法将搜索逻辑与特定问题编码分离，智能体负责动态决定何时进行局部改进（强化）及何时进行大规模跳跃（探索）。

Result: 在 CVRP 和 VRPTW 基准测试中，COAgents 表现优异。在 VRPTW 上，它设定了基于学习方法的新 SOTA，相比最强的神经求解器（如 POMO）及传统算法（如 ALNS），在不同规模的实例中显著缩小了与最优解之间的差距，表现出极强的竞争力和鲁棒性。

Conclusion: COAgents 通过将搜索过程建模为图，利用多智能体协作机制，成功克服了传统启发式算法泛化能力差及端到端学习方法在复杂约束下表现不佳的问题。该框架证明了将通用的搜索控制策略与领域特定的编码方案解耦，是提升车辆路径问题求解效率与质量的有效途径。

Abstract: Although Vehicle Routing Problems (VRP) are essential to many real-world systems, they remain computationally intractable at scale due to their combinatorial complexity. Traditional heuristics rely on handcrafted rules for local improvements and occasional \textit{jumps} to escape local minima, but often struggle to generalize across diverse instances. We introduce \textbf{COAgents}, a cooperative multi-agent framework that models the search process as a graph: nodes represent solutions, and edges correspond to either local refinements or large perturbations for diversification (i.e., jumps). A \textit{Partial Search Graph} (PSG) is dynamically constructed during search, enabling COAgents to train a Node Selection Agent and a Move Selection Agent to guide intensification, and a Jump Agent to trigger well-timed explorations of new regions. Unlike end-to-end learning approaches, COAgents cleanly separates problem-agnostic search control from compact domain-specific encoding, facilitating adaptability across tasks. Extensive experiments on the CVRP and VRPTW benchmarks show that COAgents remains competitive with several learn-to-search baselines on CVRP and sets a new state of the art among learning-based methods on the more challenging VRPTW instances, reducing the gap to the best-known solutions by 14\% at $N\!=\!100$ and 44\% at $N\!=\!50$ relative to the strongest neural solver (POMO), and by 21\% and 40\% respectively relative to ALNS.
  Code is available at https://github.com/mahdims/COAgents.

</details>

### [192] [Declarative Data Services: Structured Agentic Discovery for Composing Data Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20690)
*Shanshan Ye,Duo Lu*

Method: 提出了“声明式数据服务”（Declarative Data Services, DDS）架构。该架构定义了四个层级的类型化契约（意图、操作符 DAG、系统特定技能、运行时归因），将全局搜索分解为有界的子搜索，并建立了知识前向传递与错误反馈路由机制，利用基于反馈的“技能补丁”来优化系统组合。

Result: 在交易后端工作负载的实验中，DDS 架构表现出优于无界发现方法的收敛性能。通过引入类型化契约和反馈回路，系统能够成功解决运行时故障，并将故障转化为后续部署可引用的技能补丁，验证了该架构在处理真实世界复杂系统组合任务中的有效性。

Conclusion: DDS 架构通过引入分层的类型化契约，有效地将复杂的系统组合问题分解为受控的子搜索，从而克服了无界智能体在处理异构数据栈时的收敛性难题，为构建自动化、可信赖的数据系统组合提供了可行的路径。

Abstract: Agentic discovery has shown that LLM-driven search can find novel algorithms, designs, and code under benchmark conditions. Translating the paradigm to multi-system data backends surfaces a harder problem: the search space is heterogeneous, the verifier is whether a deployed stack actually runs, and composition knowledge is unevenly captured in pretraining. Unbounded agentic discovery, a coding agent iterating on failure-log feedback, fails to converge consistently on a working stack even when iteration and explicit composition knowledge are added. We propose Declarative Data Services (DDS), an architecture for structured agentic discovery of data-system compositions from declarative user intent. The framework owns four typed contracts at successive layers (intent, operator DAG, per-system skills, runtime attribution) that decompose the global search into bounded sub-searches; sub-agents search each typed space, while the framework provides the channels by which knowledge flows forward as inline skill citations and errors route backward as typed signals. As a proof of life on a trading-backend workload, DDS converges where unbounded discovery does not; runtime failures become skill patches that the next deployment cites inline. We position this as an early prototype reporting lessons from real-world data-system composition.

### [194] [Conflict-Aware Additive Guidance for Flow Models under Compositional Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20758)
*Xuehui Yu,Fucheng Cai,Meiyi Wang,Xiaopeng Fan,Harold Soh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对扩散与流模型在多约束引导下容易偏离数据流形的问题，本文提出了一种名为 $g^\text{car}$ 的冲突感知引导方法，通过动态校正梯度冲突，在保持高计算效率的同时显著提升了受控生成的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推理时引导方法在处理多个外部约束（如代价函数或预训练验证器）的组合时，容易导致生成轨迹偏离真实数据流形。本文旨在探究这种“偏离流形漂移”（off-manifold drift）的根本原因，并寻求一种无需微调且能同时处理多项约束的有效引导策略。

Method: 本文提出了一种名为“冲突感知加法引导”（Conflict-Aware Additive Guidance, $g^\text{car}$）的方法。该方法通过分析梯度失调与近似误差之间的缩放关系，设计了轻量级且可学习的机制，能够在推理阶段主动检测并解决多约束引导过程中产生的梯度冲突，从而确保生成轨迹保持在数据流形之内。

Result: 在合成数据集、图像编辑以及生成式决策规划等多个领域的实验证明，$g^\text{car}$ 能够有效修正偏离流形的漂移现象。相比现有基准方法，该方法在保持轻量计算开销的同时，显著提升了生成结果的忠实度（fidelity）和质量。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的冲突感知加法引导（$g^\text{car}$）通过在推理过程中动态检测并修正梯度冲突，成功解决了扩散与流模型在多约束引导下的偏离数据流形（off-manifold）问题，为复杂条件下的受控生成提供了一种高效、轻量的通用方案。

Abstract: Inference-time guided sampling steers state-of-the-art diffusion and flow models without fine-tuning by interpreting the generation process as a controllable trajectory. This provides a simple and flexible way to inject external constraints (e.g., cost functions or pre-trained verifiers) for controlled generation. However, existing methods often fail when composing multiple constraints simultaneously, which leads to deviations from the true data manifold. In this work, we identify root causes of this off-manifold drift and find that the approximation error scales severely with gradient misalignment. Building on these findings, we propose Conflict-Aware Additive Guidance ($g^\text{car}$), a lightweight and learnable method, which actively rectifies off-manifold drift by dynamically detecting and resolving gradient conflicts. We validate $g^\text{car}$ across diverse domains, ranging from synthetic datasets and image editing to generative decision-making for planning and control. Our results demonstrate that $g^\text{car}$ effectively rectifies off-manifold drift, surpassing baselines in generation fidelity while using light compute. Code is available at https://github.com/yuxuehui/CAR-guidance.

### [195] [Interaction Locality in Hierarchical Recursive Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20784)
*Yosuke Miyanishi,Tetsuro Morimura*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了“交互局部性”框架，量化并分析了递归推理模型与具身模型在空间推理过程中信息流的局部与全局动态，发现递归模型通过局部交互的累积构建全局结构，而具身模型在模块接口处处理空间局部性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间推理既需要基于位置的局部计算，也需要维持位置无关的全局结构（路径、对象或约束规划）。现有研究缺乏一种有效且统一的框架来衡量模型在处理复杂任务时，信息流是如何在局部单元与全局结构之间传递和演变的。

Method: 作者提出了“交互局部性”框架，通过稀疏自编码器（SAE）特征消融、有限噪声激活修补（Activation Patching）以及结构化雅可比矩阵和注意力分析，量化模型信息流在空间/语义上的分布情况。实验涵盖了HRM、TRM模型在Maze-Hard、Sudoku Extreme和ARC-AGI任务，以及MTU3D具身场景基础模型。

Result: 实验发现，在分层递归模型（HRM/TRM）中，高层递归状态主要在局部空间内更新信息，通过多次递归累积形成全局解。相比之下，在具身3D模型中，因果空间局部性主要集中在视觉特征向地面化模块转换的接口处，而非视觉编码器的全过程。

Conclusion: 本文提出的“交互局部性”框架成功将空间推理中“局部执行与全局规划”的直觉转化为可量化的指标，揭示了递归推理模型倾向于通过多次局部信息交互积累出全局结构，而具身模型则倾向于在模块边界处处理空间信息。

Abstract: Spatial reasoning requires both location-bound computation and location-invariant structure: agents must make local moves while preserving route, object, or constraint-level plans. We propose interaction locality, a task-geometry-aware framework for measuring whether information flow stays within nearby cells or semantic segments, or crosses them. We instantiate the framework with sparse-autoencoder feature ablations and finite-noise activation patching, with structural Jacobian and attention checks reported in the appendix, and apply it to HRM and TRM, two compact hierarchical and recursive reasoning models, on Maze-Hard, Sudoku Extreme, and ARC-AGI. Across these models, activation patching gives the clearest architectural fingerprint: high-level recurrent states tend to write information within nearby cells or same-segment units, while repeated recursive updates accumulate these local writes into broader solution structure. This pattern holds across maze paths, Sudoku constraints, and ARC-AGI object neighborhoods, with the strongest concentration in TRM. To test whether interaction locality extends beyond toy-yet-challenging grid benchmarks, we also apply it to MTU3D, a large-scale embodied 3D scene-grounding model. In this MTU3D setting, causal spatial locality appears primarily at the transition where visual scene features are handed to the downstream grounding module, rather than uniformly throughout the visual encoder. This contrast suggests that the local-to-global handoff observed in HRM and TRM is tied to explicit recursive reasoning dynamics, while embodied 3D models may concentrate causal spatial structure at module boundaries. Interaction locality turns the intuitive local-execution/global-planning story into a reproducible measurement framework for recursive and embodied spatial reasoning.

### [196] [Conditional Equivalence of DPO and RLHF: Implicit Assumption, Failure Modes, and Provable Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20834)
*Zhiqin Yang,Yonggang Zhang,Wei Xue,Dong Fang,Bo Han,Yike Guo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了DPO与RLHF在理论上的等价性存在局限，指出了DPO在特定条件下会导致模型偏向负面反馈。为此，研究者提出了约束偏好优化（CPO）方法，通过引入约束机制实现了更可靠的人类偏好对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管直接偏好优化（DPO）作为RLHF的替代方案被广泛使用，但其理论上的等价性并非普适。作者旨在揭示DPO在实际应用中因隐含假设违背而导致的性能下降问题（即模型可能倾向于生成非偏好响应），并寻求一种既保持简洁又能保证对齐效果的改进方法。

Method: 1. 对DPO与RLHF的数学等价性进行边界条件分析，指出其对“RLHF最优策略必须偏好人类首选响应”这一隐含假设的依赖。2. 通过几何视角（软间隔排序）揭示DPO在负目标下的病态表现。3. 提出约束偏好优化（CPO）方法，将RLHF目标与约束条件相结合，以确保对齐的有效性。

Result: 理论分析表明，在特定情况下DPO与RLHF优化目标不同。实验结果显示，CPO在多个标准基准测试上均达到了最先进（SOTA）的性能，有效缓解了DPO的病态收敛问题。

Conclusion: DPO的理论保证在特定条件下会失效，这会导致模型出现优化病态。研究提出的约束偏好优化（CPO）通过引入约束条件，成功解决了DPO在人类偏好对齐中的缺陷，并提供了更稳健的训练目标。

Abstract: Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) has emerged as a popular alternative to Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF), offering theoretical equivalence with simpler implementation. We prove this equivalence is conditional rather than universal, depending on an implicit assumption frequently violated in practice: the RLHF-optimal policy must prefer human-preferred responses. When this assumption fails, DPO optimizes relative advantage over the reference policy rather than absolute alignment with human preferences, leading to pathological convergence where policies decrease DPO loss while preferring dispreferred responses. We characterize when this assumption is violated, show the existence of an undesirable solution space, and prove that DPO and RLHF optimize fundamentally different objectives in such cases. To address this, we introduce Constrained Preference Optimization (CPO), augmenting RLHF with constraints for provable alignment. We further provide a geometric interpretation through soft margin ranking, revealing that DPO implements margin ranking with potentially negative targets. Our theoretical analysis establishes when DPOs' guarantees hold and provides solutions preserving simplicity with provable alignment. Comprehensive experiments on standard benchmarks demonstrate that CPO achieves state-of-the-art performance. Code is available at: https://github.com/visitworld123/CPO.

### [197] [PlanningBench: Generating Scalable and Verifiable Planning Data for Evaluating and Training Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20873)
*Ziliang Zhao,Zenan Xu,Shuting Wang,Hongjin Qian,Yan Lei,Minda Hu,Zhao Wang,Shihan Dou,Zhicheng Dou,Pluto Zhou*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 PlanningBench，这是一个用于生成可扩展、多样化且可验证规划数据的框架。它通过结构化分类体系和约束驱动的合成流水线，解决了现有基准测试数据固定、可控性差的问题，并通过实证证明该方法能有效提升大模型的规划能力与训练效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的规划基准测试多将数据视为固定的实例集合，难以实现场景的动态覆盖，且评估难度往往仅基于表层指标而非结构性本质。这种局限性阻碍了规划数据的规模化生成、自动验证及模型训练，因此需要一种能够可控地生成多样化、可验证规划数据的通用框架。

Method: 1. 构建了一个包含 30 多种任务类型、子任务及约束条件的分类体系（Taxonomy）；2. 开发了一套约束驱动的合成流水线（Constraint-driven synthesis pipeline），用于生成具备自适应难度控制、质量过滤和实例级验证检查表（Verification checklists）的规划问题；3. 将该框架用于模型评估，并通过强化学习利用生成的验证数据对模型进行训练。

Result: 1. 评估结果显示，当前前沿大模型在处理耦合约束的复杂规划任务时仍面临挑战；2. 强化学习实验表明，使用 PlanningBench 数据进行训练可显著提升模型在未见过的规划基准测试及更广泛指令遵循任务中的性能；3. 发现具备明确最优解的任务能产生更好的训练信号，使训练过程更稳定。

Conclusion: PlanningBench 提供了一个可控且可扩展的规划数据生成框架，能够有效诊断并提升大语言模型的规划能力。研究表明，利用经过验证的高质量规划数据进行强化学习，可以显著改善模型在规划任务及通用指令遵循任务中的表现。明确的最优解为训练提供了更清晰的奖励信号和更稳定的训练动态。

Abstract: Planning is a fundamental capability for large language models (LLMs) because such complex tasks require models to coordinate goals, constraints, resources, and long-term consequences into executable and verifiable solutions. Existing planning benchmarks, however, usually treat planning data as fixed collections of instances rather than controllable generation targets. This limits scenario coverage, ties difficulty to surface-level proxies rather than structural sources, and offers limited support for scalable generation, automatic verification, or planning-oriented training. We introduce PlanningBench, a framework for generating scalable, diverse, and verifiable planning data for both evaluation and training. PlanningBench starts from real planning scenarios and abstracts practical workflows into a structured taxonomy of more than 30 task types, subtasks, constraint families, and difficulty factors. Guided by this taxonomy, a constraint-driven synthesis pipeline instantiates self-contained planning problems with adaptive difficulty control, quality filtering, and instance-level verification checklists. This shifts planning data construction from fixed benchmark collection to controllable generation while preserving realistic task grounding. We use PlanningBench to evaluate open-source and closed-source frontier LLMs, and find that current models still struggle to produce complete solutions under coupled constraints. Beyond evaluation, reinforcement learning on verified PlanningBench data improves performance on unseen planning benchmarks and broader instruction-following tasks. Further analysis suggests that determinate or well-specified optimal solutions provide clearer reward signals and more stable training dynamics. Overall, PlanningBench provides a controllable source of planning data for diagnosing and improving generalizable planning abilities in LLMs.

### [198] [For How Long Should We Be Punching? Learning Action Duration in Fighting Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20911)
*Hoang Hai Nguyen,Kurt Driessens,Dennis J. N. J. Soemers*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了格斗游戏中强化学习智能体自主决策动作持续时间的方法，旨在平衡反应灵敏度与计算成本。研究发现，虽然智能体能学会动态时长决策，但相比于提高反应能力，它们更倾向于通过高延迟决策带来的简单动作重复来规避对抗难度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 格斗游戏等实时环境中，传统的固定帧率决策机制存在局限：每帧决策会导致非人的超快反应，而固定的长间隔决策则会降低系统的灵敏度。研究旨在通过让智能体自主决定动作持续时间，从而实现对响应速度的动态调节。

Method: 提出了一个联合预测动作及其执行时长的强化学习框架。智能体不仅学习“做什么”，还学习“做多久”。通过在 FightLadder 格斗游戏环境中训练，对比了不同固定帧跳过（Frame Skip）配置与该动态时长策略的性能、响应速度及行为模式。

Result: 实验显示，学习到的动态时长策略在性能上可以与经过调优的固定帧跳过策略相媲美，并能产生可重复的动作模式。然而，智能体表现最好的配置通常是高帧跳过（低响应），这主要归因于智能体倾向于通过重复动作来“利用”脚本机器人的行为漏洞，而非通过灵活的反应取胜。

Conclusion: 动态决策时长虽然在理论上能提供更灵活的反应机制，但实验表明，单纯依靠学习动作持续时间并不足以保证智能体的鲁棒性。研究发现，在对抗固定脚本机器人时，智能体倾向于选择较大的帧跳过（即低反应灵敏度），通过重复简单的动作策略来利用对手的弱点，而非发展出人类般的实时反应能力。

Abstract: Fighting games such as Street Fighter II present unique challenges to reinforcement learning (RL) agents due to their fast-paced, real-time nature. In most RL frameworks, agents are hard-coded to make decisions at a fixed interval, typically every frame or every N frames. Although this design ensures timely responses, it restricts the agent's ability to adjust its reaction timing. Acting every frame grants frame-perfect reflexes, which are unrealistic compared to human players, whereas longer fixed intervals reduce computational cost but hinder responsiveness. We consider an alternative decision-making framework in which the agent learns not only what action to take but also for how long to execute it. By jointly predicting both action and duration, the agent can dynamically adapt its responsiveness to different situations in the game. We implement this method using the open-source FightLadder environment with agents trained against scripted built-in bots, systematically testing different frame skip configurations to analyze their influence on performance, responsiveness, and learned behavior. Experiments show that learned timing can match the performance of well-chosen fixed frame skips and encourages repeatable action patterns, but does not ensure robustness on its own. In most cases, we see agents performing best with consistently high frame skip values (i.e., low responsiveness). This strategy makes it easier to learn exploitative strategies where the same action is repeated over and over, which the scripted bots appear to be susceptible to.

</details>


### [199] [Playing Devil's Advocate: Off-the-Shelf Persona Vectors Rival Targeted Steering for Sycophancy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21006)
*Ishaan Kelkar,Nebras Alam,Vikram Kakaria,Madhur Panwar,Vasu Sharma,Maheep Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究发现，通过赋予模型“怀疑”或“审视”的人格特质，可以比传统的CAA方法更有效地减轻模型的谄媚行为，且不会牺牲模型在正确回答时的准确性。这揭示了谄媚本质上更像是一种人格属性，而非单一的偏差方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对大语言模型中存在的“谄媚（sycophancy）”现象（即模型即便在用户错误时也倾向于附和用户），现有的缓解技术（如CAA）虽然有效，但可能损害模型在用户正确时的准确性。因此，研究旨在探索无需专门训练谄媚数据的现成“人格引导”技术是否能作为一种更优的替代方案。

Method: 该研究对比了传统的“对比激活添加（CAA）”方法与“现成的人格引导向量”。研究在两个指令微调模型上，通过引导模型呈现具有“怀疑”或“审视”特质的人格，观察其对谄媚行为的影响，并从几何角度分析了人格向量与谄媚方向的关系。

Result: 在实验模型中，引导向具有“怀疑”或“审视”特质的人格，能够达到CAA缓解效果的68%至98%，且在用户正确时不会导致准确率下降。此外，该效应具有非对称性，向“顺从”人格引导并不会显著增加谄媚程度。几何分析表明，人格向量与激活空间中的谄媚方向在很大程度上是相互独立的。

Conclusion: 研究表明，谄媚行为并非由单一可操纵的方向决定，而是一种更接近“人格（persona）”层面的属性。通过人格引导（如赋予模型怀疑或审视的特质）可以在保持模型准确性的同时有效缓解谄媚，且优于传统的对比激活添加（CAA）方法。

Abstract: We study the effect of different persona on \textbf{sycophancy}: model's agreement with users even when the user is incorrect. The standard mitigation, Contrastive Activation Addition (CAA), derives a steering direction from labelled pairs of sycophantic and honest responses. This study evaluates whether off-the-shelf persona steering vectors, originally developed for general role-playing and not trained on sycophancy data, can serve as an alternative. In two instruction-tuned models, steering toward personas characterised by doubt or scrutiny reduces sycophancy to approximately $68\%$ and $98\%$ of CAA's effect, and, unlike CAA, maintains accuracy when the user is correct. The effect is also asymmetric: steering toward agreeable personas does not produce a mirror increase in sycophancy. Geometrically, the persona vector is largely independent of the direction of sycophancy in activation space. Collectively, these findings suggest that sycophancy is better understood as a persona-level property rather than a single steerable direction. We release our code here: https://anonymous.4open.science/r/Sycophancy-Steering-9DF0/.

</details>


### [200] [ScenePilot: Controllable Boundary-Driven Critical Scenario Generation for Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21168)
*Qiyu Ruan,Yuxuan Wang,He Li,Zhenning Li,Cheng-zhong Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ScenePilot 是一种自动驾驶场景生成框架，通过多目标强化学习和可行性屏蔽技术，专门生成既符合物理定律又具有挑战性的测试场景，有效填补了现有压力测试方法中物理真实性与诱发故障能力之间的缺口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自动驾驶场景生成方法存在局限性：要么生成的场景因缺乏物理约束而产生“虚假”碰撞（物理上不可解），要么过分关注攻击性或受限于特定控制器的边界，导致测试不够全面。因此，作者旨在构建一种能够生成物理可解且能有效诱发自动驾驶系统失效的“边界带”场景，从而提高压力测试的有效性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ScenePilot 的框架，该框架将场景生成建模为带约束的多目标强化学习问题。其核心方法包括：1. 结合基于 RSS（责任敏感安全）的物理可行性评分 $σ$ 与在线学习的 AV（自动驾驶）风险预测器 $Φ$；2. 引入步级可行性感知屏蔽（feasibility-aware shielding）机制，确保探索过程处于物理可行的边界带内，同时过滤掉物理上不可行的异常场景。

Result: 在 SafeBench 平台上的实验结果显示，ScenePilot 生成的场景使碰撞率提升了 6.2 个百分点，同时保持了场景的物理合理性。此外，利用这些边界场景进行的对抗性微调，在多个规划器（planner）上均实现了下游事故率的持续降低。

Conclusion: ScenePilot 通过聚焦于物理可解但会导致自动驾驶系统失效的“边界带”场景，有效地提升了压力测试的质量。研究表明，在这些边界场景下进行对抗性微调，能够显著降低实际应用中的事故率，证明了该框架在提升自动驾驶安全性方面的实用价值。

Abstract: Safety-critical scenarios are central to evaluating autonomous driving systems, yet their rarity in naturalistic logs makes simulation-based stress testing indispensable. Most scenario generation methods treat surrounding agents as adversaries, but they either (i) induce failures without explicitly modeling vehicle-road physical limits, yielding visually extreme yet physically unsolvable crashes, or (ii) enforce physical feasibility or policy feasibility in isolation, which can over-focus on aggressive maneuvers or remain tied to a controller-dependent capability boundary. We propose ScenePilot, a feasibility-guided, boundary-driven framework that targets the boundary band: scenarios that are physically solvable in principle yet still cause the deployed autonomy stack to fail. We formulate generation as constrained multi-objective reinforcement learning, combining an RSS-derived physical-feasibility score $σ$ with an online-learned AV-risk predictor $Φ$, and introduce step-level feasibility-aware shielding to keep exploration near the feasibility boundary while avoiding infeasible artifacts. Experiments on SafeBench with multiple planners show that ScenePilot yields substantially higher collision rates (+6.2 percentage points) while preserving physical validity, and that adversarial fine-tuning on these boundary-band scenarios consistently reduces downstream crash rates. The code is available at https://github.com/QiyuRuan/ScenePilot.

</details>

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种有效的语料库级LLM智能体诊断方法，通过自动生成基于证据的洞察报告，显著提升了开发者定位系统性故障的能力，为智能体的迭代优化提供了可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Diagnosing failures in LLM agents remains largely manual. Practitioners inspect a small subset of execution traces, form ad-hoc hypotheses, and iterate. This process misses patterns that only emerge across trace populations and does not scale to production corpora where individual traces span tens of thousands of tokens. We formalize the problem of corpus-level trace diagnostics. Given a corpus of execution traces, the goal is to produce grounded natural-language insights that characterize systematic behavioral patterns across trace groups, each linked to supporting evidence. We present the Insights Generator (IG), a multi-agent system that answers diagnostic questions by proposing and testing hypotheses across the trace corpus to produce an evidence-backed insights report. We evaluate IG across qualitative and objective dimensions, spanning rubric-based report assessment and downstream performance improvements achieved by implementing IG insights. Human experts using IG reports improve scaffold performance by 30.4pp over the unmodified baseline scaffold, and coding agents leveraging IG-derived insights show consistent and stable gains. Across benchmarks, IG's scout-investigator architecture produces findings comparable in detection coverage to competing approaches, while domain experts rated IG reports as leading depth and evidence quality.

*Haiyang Shen,Jiuzheng Wang,Taian Guo,Mugeng Liu,Wenchun Jing,Chongyang Pan,Siqi Zhong,Zhiyang Chen,Weichen Bi,Yudong Han,Xiaoying Bai,Yun Ma*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出了一种基于课程的实践教学方法：引导学生将学科知识转化为可验证的专家级问题，通过互评设计来消除歧义，并利用这些问题对深度研究AI系统进行压力测试。最终构建了一个包含14个人文社科领域、共256个问题的基准测试集（QuestBench）。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了通过让学生参与构建基准测试（QuestBench），不仅能帮助他们识别AI系统的局限性，还能将他们从单纯的AI“使用者”转变为具备批判性思维的“知识评判者”。这种教学方法强调了在AI时代，理解学科专业知识的标准并以此评估AI输出对于培养负责任的知识主体至关重要。

Abstract: As AI becomes part of everyday learning, many courses teach students to use it mainly as a productivity tool: how to prompt, search, summarize, write, code, and use tools more efficiently. We argue that AI education also needs a setting in which students learn to test AI and understand their own role in judging machine-produced knowledge. To this end, we introduce a course-based practice that teaches AI through benchmark construction, using deep research systems as a concrete example of AI-era knowledge work. Students turn disciplinary knowledge into verifiable expert-level questions, review one another's designs for ambiguity and shortcuts, and evaluate AI systems on the resulting tasks. This activity gives students direct exposure to a powerful tool while asking them to specify what a trustworthy answer would require. The produced benchmark, QuestBench, consists of 256 questions across 14 humanities and social-science domains. Evaluation on QuestBench shows that student-designed tasks reveal hidden failures in current deep research systems: across thirteen evaluated systems, the mean question-level pass rate is only 16.85%, and the best-performing system, GPT-5.5, reaches a 57.58% pass rate. The failures are educationally useful because they show how fluent, source-backed answers can still miss the right query, source, term, or evidence standard. Reflections from five student contributors suggest that benchmark construction can help students see professional knowledge not only as content AI may retrieve, but as the basis for judging AI outputs. We present QuestBench as a benchmark artifact and as a reusable classroom setting for a larger educational question: how students can remain responsible knowledge actors as AI enters learning and professional work. The dataset is available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/PKUAIWeb/QuestBench/tree/main.

### [203] [PALS: Power-Aware LLM Serving for Mixture-of-Experts Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21427)
*Can Hankendi,Rana Shahout,Minlan Yu,Ayse K. Coskun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PALS 是一种针对 LLM 推理的功率感知运行时，通过动态调节 GPU 功率限制与批处理参数，在满足 QoS 的前提下显著提升了能效并实现了功率预算跟踪。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 LLM 推理在数据中心消耗巨大，但现有系统多将 GPU 功率视为静态约束，缺乏动态调节机制以平衡高吞吐量需求与能源效率。

Method: 提出了一种感知功率的 LLM 服务运行时 PALS，通过结合轻量级离线功耗-性能模型与反馈驱动控制器，实现 GPU 功率限制与批处理大小等软件参数的联合优化。

Result: 在 vLLM 框架中实现后，PALS 在多 GPU 系统及密集/MoE 模型上提升了高达 26.3% 的能效，在功率限制下将 QoS 违规率降低了 4 到 7 倍，并能有效跟踪动态功率预算。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) inference has become a dominant workload in modern data centers, driving significant GPU utilization and energy consumption. While prior systems optimize throughput and latency by batching, scheduling, and parallelism, they largely treat GPU power as a static constraint rather than a controllable resource. In this paper, we present a power-aware runtime for LLM serving, PALS, that treats GPU power caps as a first-class control knob and jointly optimizes them with software parameters such as batch size. The system combines lightweight offline power-performance models with a feedback-driven controller to select configurations that satisfy throughput targets while maximizing energy efficiency. We implement PALS within an existing LLM serving framework, vLLM, demonstrating that it requires no model retraining or API changes. Across multi-GPU systems and both dense and mixture-of-experts (MoE) models, PALS improves energy efficiency by up to 26.3%, reduces QoS violations by 4x to 7x under power constraints, and tracks dynamic power budgets. These results highlight the potential of integrating power control directly into LLM inference runtimes, enabling energy-proportional and grid-interactive AI systems.

### [204] [Mind the Sim-to-Real Gap & Think Like a Scientist](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21458)
*Harsh Parikh,Gabriel Levin-Konigsberg,Dominique Perrault-Joncas,Alexander Volfovsky*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了在存在偏差的模拟器与高成本真实实验之间如何进行权衡，提出了基于方差最小化的Fisher-SEP算法，通过理论证明与案例分析展示了主动实验在修正模拟偏差及拓展策略探索范围方面的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预训练模拟器虽然查询成本低，但存在校准误差和分布偏移（如混杂因素或漂移）；而真实环境实验无偏但成本高昂。研究旨在解决如何以最优方式利用模拟器并结合少量真实实验来做出可靠决策。

Method: 1. 扩展模拟引理（Extended Simulation Lemma）：将模拟器误差分解为可由随机化识别的校准-部署偏移及不可约的参数残差。
2. 值差距分解：将策略差距分为局部组件（已知状态）和可达性组件（未访问状态）。
3. Fisher-SEP 算法：提出一种仿真辅助实验策略，通过最小化目标策略价值的后验预测方差来优化实验分配。

Result: 1. 证明了在纯被动学习模式下，对于长期决策，策略的性能差距始终存在且无法消除。
2. Fisher-SEP 算法在实验设计中表现优异，尤其是在长周期任务和具有数据孤岛（如HIV移动监测案例）的场景中，能够显著提升决策的可靠性和覆盖范围。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论分析揭示了在预训练模拟器存在偏差的情况下，如何最优地结合模拟器与真实实验来优化决策策略。研究表明，仅依靠被动学习无法克服分布偏移带来的可达性挑战，而通过设计的实验（如Fisher-SEP）可以有效地识别偏差并探索模拟器未覆盖的状态空间。

Abstract: Suppose a planner has a pre-trained simulator of a sequential decision problem and the option to run real experiments in the field. The simulator is cheap to query but inherits confounding and drift from its calibration data. Experimentation is unbiased but consumes one real unit per trial. We study when, and how, the planner should supplement the simulator with experiments. We give three results. First, an extended simulation lemma decomposes the simulator's value error into a calibration--deployment shift that randomization can identify and a parametric residual that no further interaction can reduce. Second, the value gap between the simulator-optimal policy and the optimum splits into a local component, on states the deployed policy already visits, and a reachability component, on states it does not. The reachability component stays bounded away from zero at any horizon under purely passive learning. Third, we propose Fisher-SEP, a simulation-aided experimental policy (SEP) that minimizes the posterior predictive variance of a target policy's value, with reward-only and transition-only specializations. Two case studies illustrate the regimes. In a vending-machine supply chain, front-loaded experimentation overtakes posterior updating once the horizon is long enough to amortize the pilot. In an HIV mobile-testing example with a corridor that separates a well-surveilled region from a poorly-surveilled one, only designed exploration reaches the poorly-surveilled region.

</details>


### [205] [AiraXiv: An AI-Driven Open-Access Platform for Human and AI Scientists](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21481)
*Junshu Pan,Panzhong Lu,Yixuan Weng,Qiyao Sun,Fang Guo,Zijie Yang,Qiji Zhou,Yue Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 为了解决 AI 时代科研论文激增导致的学术出版系统过载问题，本文提出了 AiraXiv 平台，通过 AI 辅助的评审与迭代流程，构建了一个高效、可扩展的学术交流与出版新生态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人工智能技术导致科研产出激增，传统的学术会议及期刊出版模式在投稿量、审稿负荷及规模化扩展方面面临巨大压力，亟需一种适应 AI 时代的高效出版范式。

Method: 构建了一个名为 AiraXiv 的开放存取平台，整合了开放预印本、基于人工智能的辅助分析与评审机制以及读者反馈循环；支持通过交互式界面与人类科学家协作，并利用模型上下文协议（MCP）与 AI 智能体进行交互。

Result: 通过实际部署（如作为 ICAIS 2025 的投稿平台）验证了系统的有效性，表明 AiraXiv 能够提供快速、包容且具有可扩展性的学术基础设施。

Conclusion: AiraXiv 证明了一种去中心化、AI 赋能的出版范式在处理海量学术产出方面具有可行性，为未来学术交流提供了一个可扩展且高效的基础设施模型。

Abstract: Recent advances in artificial intelligence (AI) have accelerated the growth of both human-authored and AI-generated research outputs, placing increasing strain on traditional academic publishing systems and challenging the scalability of conference- and journal-centered paradigms amid rising submission volumes, reviewer workload, and venue size. To address these challenges, we explore an AI-era publishing paradigm in which both human and AI scientists participate as authors and readers, and papers evolve through continuous, feedback-driven iteration. We propose AiraXiv, an AI-driven open-access platform built on open preprints, AI-augmented analysis and review, and reader feedback. AiraXiv supports human scientists through an interactive UI and AI scientists through Model Context Protocol (MCP)-based interactions. We validate AiraXiv through real-world deployments, including serving as the submission platform for ICAIS 2025, demonstrating its potential as a fast, inclusive, and scalable research infrastructure for the AI era. AiraXiv is publicly available at https://airaxiv.com.

</details>


### [206] [DeepWeb-Bench: A Deep Research Benchmark Demanding Massive Cross-Source Evidence and Long-Horizon Derivation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21482)
*Sixiong Xie,Zhuofan Shi,Haiyang Shen,Jiuzheng Wang,Siqi Zhong,Mugeng Liu,Chongyang Pan,Peilun Jia,Baoqing Sun,Xiang Jing,Yun Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了DeepWeb-Bench基准以测试AI模型的深度研究能力。研究指出模型的主要短板在于推理和校准而非检索，且不同模型在复杂任务中表现出显著的性能差异与领域特异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的深度研究基准过于简单，难以有效区分前沿语言模型在处理复杂、长程、多来源信息任务时的真实能力差异，因此需要构建一个更具挑战性的评估框架。

Method: 研究团队提出了DeepWeb-Bench基准，该基准包含需要大规模证据收集、跨来源整合及长程多步推导的任务。研究从检索、推导、推理和校准四个维度对9个前沿模型进行了评估，并利用具有溯源记录的参考答案对模型输出进行了严格的审计与定量分析。

Result: 实验发现：1. 检索并非主要瓶颈（仅占错误的12-14%），推导与校准失败占70%以上；2. 强模型常因推导不完整出错，弱模型则倾向于虚构精确性；3. 模型间存在显著的领域特异性，不同模型在同一任务上的结果一致性较低（ρ=0.61）。

Conclusion: DeepWeb-Bench揭示了当前模型在深度研究任务中的真实瓶颈并非检索，而是推理和校准能力。研究发现，强模型与弱模型的失败模式存在本质区别，且不同模型在特定领域表现出显著的专业化差异，这为未来提升AI深度研究能力提供了明确的优化方向。

Abstract: Deep research, in which an agent searches the open web, collects evidence, and derives an answer through extended reasoning, is a prominent use case for frontier language models. Frontier deep research products score high on existing benchmarks, making it difficult to distinguish their capabilities from current evaluation data alone. We introduce DeepWeb-Bench, a deep research benchmark that is substantially harder than existing benchmarks for the current frontier. Difficulty comes from three properties of the data itself: each task requires massive evidence collection, cross-source reconciliation, and long-horizon multi-step derivation. We represent these three sources of difficulty as four capability families (Retrieval, Derivation, Reasoning, and Calibration) and report results sliced by family. Every reference answer is accompanied by a source-provenance record with four disclosure levels and cross-source checks where available, making scores easier to audit against the underlying evidence. We evaluate DeepWeb-Bench on nine frontier models and report three findings: (1) retrieval is not the bottleneck, as retrieval failures account for only 12-14% of errors while derivation and calibration failures account for over 70%; (2) strong and weak models fail in qualitatively different ways, with strong models' errors dominated by incomplete derivation and weak models' by hallucinated precision; and (3) models exhibit genuine specialization across domains, with cross-model agreement of only rho = 0.61 and per-case disagreement reaching 18.8 percentage points. The public benchmark release includes the data, rubrics, and evaluation code.

</details>
